1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. import * as esbuild from 'esbuild';
3. import { promises as fs } from 'fs';
4. import path from 'path';
5. import { fileURLToPath } from 'url';
6. import { polyfillNode } from 'esbuild-plugin-polyfill-node';
7. 
8. const __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));
9. 
10. const isWatch = process.argv.includes('--watch');
11. 
12. async function copyDir(src, dest) {
13.   await fs.mkdir(dest, { recursive: true });
14.   const entries = await fs.readdir(src, { withFileTypes: true });
15. 
16.   for (const entry of entries) {
17.     const srcPath = path.join(src, entry.name);
18.     const destPath = path.join(dest, entry.name);
19. 
20.     if (entry.isDirectory()) {
21.       await copyDir(srcPath, destPath);
22.     } else {
23.       await fs.copyFile(srcPath, destPath);
24.     }
25.   }
26. }
27. 
28. async function build() {
29.   const manifestPath = path.join(__dirname, 'src/manifest.json');
30.   const manifestContent = await fs.readFile(manifestPath, 'utf8');
31.   const manifest = JSON.parse(manifestContent);
32.   const version = manifest.version;
33. 
34.   console.log(`рҹ”Ё Building TiltCheck Browser Extension v${version}...`);
35. 
36.   // Clean dist directory (but preserve icons if they exist)
37.   const distPath = path.join(__dirname, 'dist');
38.   const iconsPath = path.join(distPath, 'icons');
39. 
40.   // Check if icons exist before cleaning
41.   let hasIcons = false;
42.   try {
43.     await fs.access(iconsPath);
44.     hasIcons = true;
45.   } catch {
46.     hasIcons = false;
47.   }
48. 
49.   await fs.rm(distPath, { recursive: true, force: true });
50.   await fs.mkdir(distPath, { recursive: true });
51. 
52.   // Build content script
53.   await esbuild.build({
54.     entryPoints: [path.join(__dirname, 'src/content.ts')],
55.     bundle: true,
56.     outfile: path.join(__dirname, 'dist/content.js'),
57.     format: 'iife',
58.     platform: 'browser',
59.     target: 'chrome100',
60.     sourcemap: true,
61.     minify: false,
62.     plugins: [],
63.     alias: {
64.       crypto: 'crypto-browserify',
65.       stream: 'stream-browserify',
66.       vm: 'vm-browserify',
67.       buffer: 'buffer',
68.     },
69.     define: {
70.       global: 'window',
71.       process: '{"env":{}}',
72.     },
73.   });
74. 
75.   // Build page-bridge script (runs in MAIN world for wallet access)
76.   await esbuild.build({
77.     entryPoints: [path.join(__dirname, 'src/page-bridge.ts')],
78.     bundle: true,
79.     outfile: path.join(__dirname, 'dist/page-bridge.js'),
80.     format: 'iife',
81.     platform: 'browser',
82.     target: 'chrome100',
83.     sourcemap: true,
84.     minify: false,
85.     plugins: [],
86.   });
87. 
88.   // Copy static files
89.   const staticFiles = [
90.     { src: 'src/manifest.json', dest: 'dist/manifest.json' },
91.     { src: 'src/background.js', dest: 'dist/background.js' },
92.     { src: 'src/auth-bridge.html', dest: 'dist/auth-bridge.html' },
93.     { src: 'src/auth-bridge.js', dest: 'dist/auth-bridge.js' },
94.   ];
95. 
96.   for (const file of staticFiles) {
97.     const srcPath = path.join(__dirname, file.src);
98.     const destPath = path.join(__dirname, file.dest);
99.     await fs.copyFile(srcPath, destPath);
100.     console.log(`рҹ“Ӣ Copied ${file.src} -> ${file.dest}`);
101.   }
102. 
103.   // Copy icons directory if it exists in src/icons
104.   const srcIconsDir = path.join(__dirname, 'src', 'icons');
105.   const destIconsDir = path.join(__dirname, 'dist', 'icons');
106.   try {
107.     await fs.access(srcIconsDir);
108.     await copyDir(srcIconsDir, destIconsDir);
109.     console.log('рҹ“Ұ Copied icons from src/icons to dist/icons');
110.   } catch {
111.     // Create icons directory and add placeholder info
112.     await fs.mkdir(destIconsDir, { recursive: true });
113.     console.log('вҡ пёҸ  Icons directory created - please add icon16.png, icon48.png, icon128.png to src/icons');
114.   }
115. 
116.   console.log('вң… Build complete! Extension ready in ./dist');
117.   console.log('');
118.   console.log('рҹ“Ұ To install in Chrome:');
119.   console.log('   1. Open chrome://extensions/');
120.   console.log('   2. Enable "Developer mode" (top right)');
121.   console.log('   3. Click "Load unpacked"');
122.   console.log('   4. Select the ./dist folder');
123.   console.log('');
124.   console.log('рҹ“Ұ To create zip:');
125.   console.log('   npm run zip');
126.   console.log('');
127. }

130.   console.error('вқҢ Build failed:', err);

1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. /**
3.  * @tiltcheck/auth - Discord OAuth Module
4.  * Discord OAuth2 authentication and user verification
5.  */
6. 
7. import type { 
8.   DiscordOAuthConfig, 
9.   DiscordUser, 
10.   DiscordTokens, 
11.   DiscordVerifyResult 
12. } from './types.js';
13. 
14. /**
15.  * Discord API endpoints
16.  */
17. const DISCORD_API_BASE = 'https://discord.com/api/v10';
18. const DISCORD_OAUTH_AUTHORIZE = 'https://discord.com/oauth2/authorize';
19. const DISCORD_OAUTH_TOKEN = `${DISCORD_API_BASE}/oauth2/token`;
20. const DISCORD_USER_ME = `${DISCORD_API_BASE}/users/@me`;
21. 
22. /**
23.  * Default OAuth scopes for TiltCheck
24.  */
25. export const DEFAULT_SCOPES = ['identify', 'identify.premium'];
26. 
27. /**
28.  * Generate Discord OAuth2 authorization URL
29.  */
30. export function getAuthorizationUrl(
31.   config: DiscordOAuthConfig,
32.   state?: string
33. ): string {
34.   const params = new URLSearchParams({
35.     client_id: config.clientId,
36.     redirect_uri: config.redirectUri,
37.     response_type: 'code',
38.     scope: config.scopes.join(' '),
39.   });
40.   
41.   if (state) {
42.     params.set('state', state);
43.   }
44.   
45.   return `${DISCORD_OAUTH_AUTHORIZE}?${params.toString()}`;
46. }
47. 
48. /**
49.  * Exchange authorization code for tokens
50.  */
51. export async function exchangeCode(
52.   code: string,
53.   config: DiscordOAuthConfig
54. ): Promise<{ success: boolean; tokens?: DiscordTokens; error?: string }> {
55.   try {
56.     const response = await fetch(DISCORD_OAUTH_TOKEN, {
57.       method: 'POST',
58.       headers: {
59.         'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
60.       },
61.       body: new URLSearchParams({
62.         client_id: config.clientId,
63.         client_secret: config.clientSecret,
64.         grant_type: 'authorization_code',
65.         code,
66.         redirect_uri: config.redirectUri,
67.       }),
68.     });
69.     
70.     if (!response.ok) {
71.       const error = await response.text();
72.       return { success: false, error: `Token exchange failed: ${error}` };
73.     }
74.     
75.     const data = await response.json() as {
76.       access_token: string;
77.       refresh_token: string;
78.       token_type: string;
79.       expires_in: number;
80.       scope: string;
81.     };
82.     
83.     return {
84.       success: true,
85.       tokens: {
86.         accessToken: data.access_token,
87.         refreshToken: data.refresh_token,
88.         tokenType: data.token_type,
89.         expiresIn: data.expires_in,
90.         scope: data.scope,
91.       },
92.     };
93.   } catch (error) {
94.     const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error';
95.     return { success: false, error: message };
96.   }
97. }
98. 
99. /**
100.  * Refresh Discord access token
101.  */
102. export async function refreshTokens(
103.   refreshToken: string,
104.   config: DiscordOAuthConfig
105. ): Promise<{ success: boolean; tokens?: DiscordTokens; error?: string }> {
106.   try {
107.     const response = await fetch(DISCORD_OAUTH_TOKEN, {
108.       method: 'POST',
109.       headers: {
110.         'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
111.       },
112.       body: new URLSearchParams({
113.         client_id: config.clientId,
114.         client_secret: config.clientSecret,
115.         grant_type: 'refresh_token',
116.         refresh_token: refreshToken,
117.       }),
118.     });
119.     
120.     if (!response.ok) {
121.       const error = await response.text();
122.       return { success: false, error: `Token refresh failed: ${error}` };
123.     }
124.     
125.     const data = await response.json() as {
126.       access_token: string;
127.       refresh_token: string;
128.       token_type: string;
129.       expires_in: number;
130.       scope: string;
131.     };
132.     
133.     return {
134.       success: true,
135.       tokens: {
136.         accessToken: data.access_token,
137.         refreshToken: data.refresh_token,
138.         tokenType: data.token_type,
139.         expiresIn: data.expires_in,
140.         scope: data.scope,
141.       },
142.     };
143.   } catch (error) {
144.     const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error';
145.     return { success: false, error: message };
146.   }
147. }
148. 
149. /**
150.  * Get Discord user info from access token
151.  */
152. export async function getDiscordUser(
153.   accessToken: string
154. ): Promise<{ success: boolean; user?: DiscordUser; error?: string }> {
155.   try {
156.     const response = await fetch(DISCORD_USER_ME, {
157.       headers: {
158.         Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}`,
159.       },
160.     });
161.     
162.     if (!response.ok) {
163.       const error = await response.text();
164.       return { success: false, error: `Failed to get user: ${error}` };
165.     }
166.     
167.     const data = await response.json() as {
168.       id: string;
169.       username: string;
170.       discriminator: string;
171.       global_name?: string;
172.       avatar?: string;
173.       email?: string;
174.       verified?: boolean;
175.       flags?: number;
176.       premium_type?: number;
177.     };
178.     
179.     return {
180.       success: true,
181.       user: {
182.         id: data.id,
183.         username: data.username,
184.         discriminator: data.discriminator,
185.         globalName: data.global_name,
186.         avatar: data.avatar,
187.         email: data.email,
188.         verified: data.verified,
189.         flags: data.flags,
190.         premiumType: data.premium_type,
191.       },
192.     };
193.   } catch (error) {
194.     const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error';
195.     return { success: false, error: message };
196.   }
197. }
198. 
199. /**
200.  * Verify Discord OAuth callback and get user info
201.  * This is the main function to use in OAuth callback handlers
202.  */
203. export async function verifyDiscordOAuth(
204.   code: string,
205.   config: DiscordOAuthConfig
206. ): Promise<DiscordVerifyResult> {
207.   // Exchange code for tokens
208.   const tokenResult = await exchangeCode(code, config);
209.   
210.   if (!tokenResult.success || !tokenResult.tokens) {
211.     return {
212.       valid: false,
213.       error: tokenResult.error || 'Failed to exchange code',
214.     };
215.   }
216.   
217.   // Get user info
218.   const userResult = await getDiscordUser(tokenResult.tokens.accessToken);
219.   
220.   if (!userResult.success || !userResult.user) {
221.     return {
222.       valid: false,
223.       error: userResult.error || 'Failed to get user info',
224.     };
225.   }
226.   
227.   return {
228.     valid: true,
229.     user: userResult.user,
230.     tokens: tokenResult.tokens,
231.   };
232. }
233. 
234. /**
235.  * Revoke Discord token
236.  */
237. export async function revokeToken(
238.   token: string,
239.   config: DiscordOAuthConfig
240. ): Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }> {
241.   try {
242.     const response = await fetch(`${DISCORD_API_BASE}/oauth2/token/revoke`, {
243.       method: 'POST',
244.       headers: {
245.         'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
246.       },
247.       body: new URLSearchParams({
248.         client_id: config.clientId,
249.         client_secret: config.clientSecret,
250.         token,
251.       }),
252.     });
253.     
254.     if (!response.ok) {
255.       const error = await response.text();
256.       return { success: false, error: `Token revocation failed: ${error}` };
257.     }
258.     
259.     return { success: true };
260.   } catch (error) {
261.     const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error';
262.     return { success: false, error: message };
263.   }
264. }
265. 
266. /**
267.  * Generate Discord avatar URL
268.  */
269. export function getAvatarUrl(user: DiscordUser, size: number = 128): string {
270.   if (user.avatar) {
271.     const extension = user.avatar.startsWith('a_') ? 'gif' : 'png';
272.     return `https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/${user.id}/${user.avatar}.${extension}?size=${size}`;
273.   }
274.   
275.   // Default avatar based on discriminator or user ID
276.   const defaultIndex = user.discriminator === '0' 
277.     ? (BigInt(user.id) >> 22n) % 6n 
278.     : parseInt(user.discriminator, 10) % 5;
279.   
280.   return `https://cdn.discordapp.com/embed/avatars/${defaultIndex}.png`;
281. }
282. 
283. /**
284.  * Generate a random state parameter for OAuth
285.  */
286. export function generateState(): string {
287.   const array = new Uint8Array(32);
288.   crypto.getRandomValues(array);
289.   return Array.from(array, (byte) => byte.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('');
290. }
291. 
292. export type { DiscordOAuthConfig, DiscordUser, DiscordTokens, DiscordVerifyResult };
293.
```

1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. (() => {
3.   const statusEl = document.getElementById('status');
4.   const openBtn = document.getElementById('open-btn');
5.   const closeBtn = document.getElementById('close-btn');
6. 
7.   const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
8.   const authUrl = params.get('authUrl');
9.   const allowedOrigins = new Set(['https://api.tiltcheck.me', 'http://localhost', 'http://127.0.0.1']);
10.   const apiOrigin = (() => {
11.     try {
12.       const origin = new URL(authUrl || 'https://api.tiltcheck.me').origin;
13.       return allowedOrigins.has(origin) ? origin : 'https://api.tiltcheck.me';
14.     } catch {
15.       return 'https://api.tiltcheck.me';
16.     }
17.   })();
18. 
19.   let popupWindow = null;
20.   let authCompleted = false;
21. 
22.   function setStatus(message) {
23.     if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = message;
24.   }
25. 
26.   function openAuthPopup() {
27.     if (!authUrl) {
28.       setStatus('Missing auth URL. Close this tab and retry from TiltCheck sidebar.');
29.       return;
30.     }
31.     let parsed;
32.     try {
33.       parsed = new URL(authUrl);
34.     } catch {
35.       setStatus('Invalid auth URL. Close this tab and retry from TiltCheck sidebar.');
36.       return;
37.     }
38.     if (!allowedOrigins.has(parsed.origin) || parsed.pathname !== '/auth/discord/login') {
39.       setStatus('Blocked unexpected auth URL. Retry from TiltCheck sidebar.');
40.       return;
41.     }
42. 
43.     popupWindow = window.open(authUrl, '_blank', 'popup=yes,width=520,height=760');
44.     if (!popupWindow) {
45.       setStatus('Popup blocked. Click "Open Discord Auth" and allow popups for this extension page.');
46.       return;
47.     }
48. 
49.     setStatus('Waiting for Discord auth confirmation...');
50.   }
51. 
52.   window.addEventListener('message', (event) => {
53.     if (authCompleted) return;
54.     if (event.origin !== apiOrigin) return;
55.     const data = event.data || {};
56.     if (data.type !== 'discord-auth' || typeof data.token !== 'string' || !data.user) return;
57. 
58.     authCompleted = true;
59.     chrome.storage.local.set(
60.       {
61.         authToken: data.token,
62.         userData: data.user,
63.       },
64.       () => {
65.         if (chrome.runtime?.lastError) {
66.           setStatus('Auth received but could not save session. Retry Connect Discord.');
67.           return;
68.         }
69. 
70.         setStatus('Discord connected. You can return to your casino tab.');
71.         try {
72.           if (popupWindow && !popupWindow.closed) popupWindow.close();
73.         } catch {
74.           // noop
75.         }
76.         setTimeout(() => window.close(), 1200);
77.       }
78.     );
79.   });
80. 
81.   openBtn?.addEventListener('click', openAuthPopup);
82.   closeBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => window.close());
83. 
84.   openAuthPopup();
85. })();
86. 
87. 
88.
```

1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. /**
3.  * @tiltcheck/auth - Cookie Session Module
4.  * Cookie-based session management with JWT tokens
5.  * All cookies: Secure, HttpOnly, SameSite=Lax, Domain=.tiltcheck.me
6.  */
7. 
8. import type { 
9.   CookieConfig, 
10.   CookieOptions, 
11.   SessionData, 
12.   SessionType,
13.   JWTConfig 
14. } from './types.js';
15. import { createToken, verifyToken } from './jwt.js';
16. 
17. /**
18.  * Default cookie configuration for TiltCheck
19.  */
20. export const DEFAULT_COOKIE_CONFIG: CookieConfig = {
21.   name: 'tiltcheck_session',
22.   domain: '.tiltcheck.me',
23.   path: '/',
24.   secure: true,
25.   httpOnly: true,
26.   sameSite: 'lax',
27.   maxAge: 7 * 24 * 60 * 60, // 7 days in seconds
28. };
29. 
30. /**
31.  * Cookie configuration for development (localhost)
32.  */
33. export const DEV_COOKIE_CONFIG: CookieConfig = {
34.   ...DEFAULT_COOKIE_CONFIG,
35.   domain: 'localhost',
36.   secure: false, // Allow HTTP in development
37. };
38. 
39. /**
40.  * Get the appropriate cookie config based on environment
41.  */
42. export function getCookieConfig(isDev?: boolean): CookieConfig {
43.   if (isDev ?? process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development') {
44.     return DEV_COOKIE_CONFIG;
45.   }
46.   return DEFAULT_COOKIE_CONFIG;
47. }
48. 
49. /**
50.  * Serialize cookie options to a Set-Cookie header string
51.  */
52. export function serializeCookie(
53.   name: string,
54.   value: string,
55.   options: CookieOptions = {}
56. ): string {
57.   const config = getCookieConfig();
58.   const mergedOptions = { ...config, ...options };
59.   
60.   const parts = [`${encodeURIComponent(name)}=${encodeURIComponent(value)}`];
61.   
62.   if (mergedOptions.domain) {
63.     parts.push(`Domain=${mergedOptions.domain}`);
64.   }
65.   
66.   if (mergedOptions.path) {
67.     parts.push(`Path=${mergedOptions.path}`);
68.   }
69.   
70.   if (mergedOptions.maxAge !== undefined) {
71.     parts.push(`Max-Age=${mergedOptions.maxAge}`);
72.   }
73.   
74.   if (mergedOptions.expires) {
75.     parts.push(`Expires=${mergedOptions.expires.toUTCString()}`);
76.   }
77.   
78.   if (mergedOptions.secure) {
79.     parts.push('Secure');
80.   }
81.   
82.   if (mergedOptions.httpOnly) {
83.     parts.push('HttpOnly');
84.   }
85.   
86.   if (mergedOptions.sameSite) {
87.     parts.push(`SameSite=${mergedOptions.sameSite.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + mergedOptions.sameSite.slice(1)}`);
88.   }
89.   
90.   return parts.join('; ');
91. }
92. 
93. /**
94.  * Parse cookies from a Cookie header string
95.  */
96. export function parseCookies(cookieHeader: string | undefined): Record<string, string> {
97.   if (!cookieHeader) {
98.     return {};
99.   }
100.   
101.   const cookies: Record<string, string> = {};
102.   
103.   cookieHeader.split(';').forEach((cookie) => {
104.     const [name, ...valueParts] = cookie.trim().split('=');
105.     if (name) {
106.       cookies[decodeURIComponent(name.trim())] = decodeURIComponent(valueParts.join('=').trim());
107.     }
108.   });
109.   
110.   return cookies;
111. }
112. 
113. /**
114.  * Create a session and return the cookie header value
115.  */
116. export async function createSession(
117.   userId: string,
118.   jwtConfig: JWTConfig,
119.   sessionData?: Partial<Omit<SessionData, 'userId' | 'createdAt'>>,
120.   cookieOptions?: Partial<CookieOptions>
121. ): Promise<{ token: string; cookie: string; sessionData: SessionData }> {
122.   const config = getCookieConfig();
123.   const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
124.   
125.   const fullSessionData: SessionData = {
126.     userId,
127.     type: sessionData?.type || 'user',
128.     discordId: sessionData?.discordId,
129.     discordUsername: sessionData?.discordUsername,
130.     walletAddress: sessionData?.walletAddress,
131.     roles: sessionData?.roles || [],
132.     createdAt: now,
133.   };
134.   
135.   // Create JWT with session data
136.   const token = await createToken(
137.     {
138.       sub: userId,
139.       type: fullSessionData.type,
140.       roles: fullSessionData.roles,
141.       discordId: fullSessionData.discordId,
142.       discordUsername: fullSessionData.discordUsername,
143.       walletAddress: fullSessionData.walletAddress,
144.     },
145.     jwtConfig
146.   );
147.   
148.   // Create cookie header
149.   const cookie = serializeCookie(config.name, token, {
150.     ...config,
151.     ...cookieOptions,
152.   });
153.   
154.   return { token, cookie, sessionData: fullSessionData };
155. }
156. 
157. /**
158.  * Destroy session by returning an expired cookie header
159.  */
160. export function destroySession(cookieOptions?: Partial<CookieOptions>): string {
161.   const config = getCookieConfig();
162.   
163.   return serializeCookie(config.name, '', {
164.     ...config,
165.     ...cookieOptions,
166.     maxAge: 0,
167.     expires: new Date(0),
168.   });
169. }
170. 
171. /**
172.  * Verify a session cookie and return the session data
173.  */
174. export async function verifySessionCookie(
175.   cookieHeader: string | undefined,
176.   jwtConfig: JWTConfig,
177.   cookieName?: string
178. ): Promise<{ valid: boolean; session?: SessionData; error?: string }> {
179.   const config = getCookieConfig();
180.   const name = cookieName || config.name;
181.   
182.   const cookies = parseCookies(cookieHeader);
183.   const token = cookies[name];
184.   
185.   if (!token) {
186.     return { valid: false, error: 'Session cookie not found' };
187.   }
188.   
189.   const result = await verifyToken(token, jwtConfig);
190.   
191.   if (!result.valid || !result.payload) {
192.     return { valid: false, error: result.error || 'Invalid session token' };
193.   }
194.   
195.   const session: SessionData = {
196.     userId: result.payload.sub,
197.     type: result.payload.type as SessionType,
198.     discordId: result.payload.discordId as string | undefined,
199.     discordUsername: result.payload.discordUsername as string | undefined,
200.     walletAddress: result.payload.walletAddress as string | undefined,
201.     roles: result.payload.roles || [],
202.     createdAt: result.payload.iat,
203.   };
204.   
205.   return { valid: true, session };
206. }
207. 
208. /**
209.  * Extract session token from cookie header
210.  */
211. export function extractSessionToken(
212.   cookieHeader: string | undefined,
213.   cookieName?: string
214. ): string | null {
215.   const config = getCookieConfig();
216.   const name = cookieName || config.name;
217.   const cookies = parseCookies(cookieHeader);
218.   return cookies[name] || null;
219. }
220. 
221. /**
222.  * Refresh a session (create new token with extended expiry)
223.  */
224. export async function refreshSession(
225.   cookieHeader: string | undefined,
226.   jwtConfig: JWTConfig,
227.   cookieName?: string
228. ): Promise<{ valid: boolean; cookie?: string; session?: SessionData; error?: string }> {
229.   const verification = await verifySessionCookie(cookieHeader, jwtConfig, cookieName);
230.   
231.   if (!verification.valid || !verification.session) {
232.     return { valid: false, error: verification.error };
233.   }
234.   
235.   // Create new session with same data but fresh token
236.   const { cookie, sessionData } = await createSession(
237.     verification.session.userId,
238.     jwtConfig,
239.     verification.session
240.   );
241.   
242.   return { valid: true, cookie, session: sessionData };
243. }
244. 
245. export type { CookieConfig, CookieOptions, SessionData };
246.
```

12.     DISCORD_SCOPES: ['identify', 'identify.premium'],

15. };
16. /**
17.  * Generate the Discord Login URL
18.  */
19. export function getDiscordLoginUrl(source = 'extension') {
20.     const url = new URL(`${EXT_CONFIG.API_BASE_URL}/auth/discord/login`);
21.     // The API handles OAuth + callback and posts a message back to the extension window.
22.     url.searchParams.set('source', source);
23.     if (source === 'extension') {
24.         // Content scripts run on page origins, so derive extension origin from runtime id.
25.         const runtimeId = typeof chrome !== 'undefined' ? chrome.runtime?.id : undefined;
26.         if (runtimeId) {
27.             url.searchParams.set('opener_origin', `chrome-extension://${runtimeId}`);
28.         }
29.     }
30.     // Preserve the caller info for debugging/analytics (not required by API).
31.     if (source && source !== 'extension') {
32.         url.searchParams.set('source_detail', source);
33.     }
34.     return url.toString();
35. }

146. const authLimiter = rateLimit({

171.   if (!secret) {

173.   }

180. function generateJWT(userId: string, email: string, roles: string[]): string {

186.     { expiresIn: '7d' }
187.   );

196.

200.     const isLocalDev =

202.       (host === 'localhost' || host === '127.0.0.1');
203.

214. /**
215.  * POST /auth/register
216.  * Register a new user with email and password
217.  */
218. router.post('/register', authLimiter, async (req, res) => {
219.   try {
220.     const { email, password } = req.body;
221. 
222.     // Validate input
223.     if (!email || !password) {
224.       res.status(400).json({
225.         error: 'Email and password are required',
226.         code: 'MISSING_FIELDS'
227.       });
228.       return;
229.     }
230. 
231.     // Validate email format
232.     const emailRegex = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
233.     if (!emailRegex.test(email)) {
234.       res.status(400).json({
235.         error: 'Invalid email format',
236.         code: 'INVALID_EMAIL'
237.       });
238.       return;
239.     }
240. 
241.     // Validate password length
242.     if (password.length < 6) {
243.       res.status(400).json({
244.         error: 'Password must be at least 6 characters',
245.         code: 'INVALID_PASSWORD'
246.       });
247.       return;
248.     }
249. 
250.     // Check if user already exists
```

392. router.get('/discord/login', authLimiter, (req, res) => {

395.     const source = req.query.source as string | undefined;
396.     const config: DiscordOAuthConfig = {
397.       ...baseConfig,
398.       redirectUri: resolveDiscordRedirectUriForSource(baseConfig, source, req),
399.     };
400. 
401.     if (!config.clientId) {
402.       res.status(500).json({ error: 'Discord OAuth not configured' });
403.       return;
404.     }

406.     // Compatibility bridge:
407.     // If Discord is configured to redirect to /discord/login, forward code/state to callback.
408.     const callbackCode = typeof req.query.code === 'string' ? req.query.code : undefined;
409.     const callbackState = typeof req.query.state === 'string' ? req.query.state : undefined;
410.     if (callbackCode || callbackState || typeof req.query.error === 'string') {
411.       const callbackParams = new URLSearchParams();
412.       if (callbackCode) callbackParams.set('code', callbackCode);
413.       if (callbackState) callbackParams.set('state', callbackState);
414.       if (typeof req.query.error === 'string') callbackParams.set('error', req.query.error);
415.       if (typeof req.query.error_description === 'string') {
416.         callbackParams.set('error_description', req.query.error_description);
417.       }
418.       const suffix = callbackParams.toString();
419.       res.redirect(`/auth/discord/callback${suffix ? `?${suffix}` : ''}`);
420.       return;
421.     }
422. 
423.     // Generate state for CSRF protection. Prefix helps recover source in callback if cookies are blocked.
424.     const statePrefix = source === 'extension' ? 'ext_' : 'web_';
425.     const state = `${statePrefix}${generateOAuthState()}`;
426. 
427.     // Store state in a short-lived cookie
428.     res.cookie('oauth_state', state, {
429.       httpOnly: true,
430.       secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
431.       sameSite: 'lax',
432.       maxAge: 10 * 60 * 1000, // 10 minutes
433.     });

442.         maxAge: 10 * 60 * 1000,
443.       });
444.     }

447.     if (source) {

451.         sameSite: 'lax',
452.         maxAge: 10 * 60 * 1000,

475. /**
476.  * GET /auth/discord/callback
477.  * Handles Discord OAuth callback
478.  */
479. router.get('/discord/callback', authLimiter, async (req, res) => {
480.   const source = getOAuthSource(req);
481.   try {
482.     const { code, state } = req.query;
483.     const storedState = req.cookies?.oauth_state;
484.     const stateValue = typeof state === 'string' ? state : '';
485.     const sourceFromState = stateValue.startsWith('ext_')
486.       ? 'extension'
487.       : stateValue.startsWith('web_')
488.         ? 'web'
489.         : undefined;
490.     const sourceFromCookie = req.cookies?.oauth_source;
491.     const isLocalDev =
492.       process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production' &&
493.       (req.hostname === 'localhost' || req.hostname === '127.0.0.1');
494. 
495.     // Optional integrity check: if both exist, cookie source must match state source.
496.     if (sourceFromCookie && sourceFromState && sourceFromCookie !== sourceFromState) {
497.       res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid OAuth source' });
498.       return;
499.     }
500. 
501.     // Verify state:
502.     // - normal: query state must match cookie
503.     // - local extension fallback: allow if state cookie is missing and state itself indicates extension source
504.     const stateValid =
505.       !!stateValue &&
506.       (stateValue === storedState || (!storedState && isLocalDev && sourceFromState === 'extension'));
507. 
508.     if (!stateValid) {
509.       res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid OAuth state' });
510.       return;
511.     }
512. 
513.     // Clear state cookie
514.     res.clearCookie('oauth_state');
515. 
516.     if (!code || typeof code !== 'string') {
517.       if (source === 'extension') {
518.         res.status(400).send(renderExtensionAuthErrorPage('Missing authorization code from Discord. Please retry.'));
519.         return;
520.       }
521.       res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing authorization code' });
522.       return;
523.     }
524. 
525.     const baseDiscordConfig = getDiscordConfig();
526.     const discordConfig: DiscordOAuthConfig = {
527.       ...baseDiscordConfig,
528.       redirectUri: resolveDiscordRedirectUriForSource(baseDiscordConfig, source, req),
529.     };
530.     const jwtConfig = getJWTConfig();
531. 
532.     // Exchange code for tokens and get user info
533.     const result = await verifyDiscordOAuth(code, discordConfig);
534. 
535.     if (!result.valid || !result.user) {
536.       if (source === 'extension') {
537.         res
538.           .status(401)
539.           .send(renderExtensionAuthErrorPage(result.error || 'Discord authentication failed. Please retry.'));
540.         return;
541.       }
542.       res.status(401).json({ error: result.error || 'Discord authentication failed' });
543.       return;
544.     }

551.     );
552.

554.     const { cookie } = await createSession(user.id, jwtConfig, {
555.       type: 'user',
556.       discordId: result.user.id,
557.       discordUsername: result.user.username,
558.       roles: user.roles,

563. 
564.     // Check if source was extension
565.     res.clearCookie('oauth_source');

567.     res.clearCookie('oauth_opener_origin');

647. /**
648.  * POST /auth/discord/activity/token
649.  * Exchange Discord Activity OAuth code for access token.
650.  *
651.  * Threat/risk notes:
652.  * - Redirect URI is validated against trusted hosts.
653.  * - Discord client secret is only used server-side.
654.  * - Errors are sanitized for clients.
655.  */
656. router.post('/discord/activity/token', activityTokenLimiter, async (req, res) => {
657.   try {
658.     const code = typeof req.body?.code === 'string' ? req.body.code.trim() : '';
659.     const redirectUriInput =
660.       typeof req.body?.redirectUri === 'string' ? req.body.redirectUri.trim() : '';
661. 
662.     if (!code || code.length < 8 || code.length > 2048) {
663.       res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid authorization code', code: 'INVALID_CODE' });
664.       return;
665.     }
666. 
667.     if (redirectUriInput && !isAllowedActivityRedirectUri(redirectUriInput)) {
668.       res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid redirect URI', code: 'INVALID_REDIRECT_URI' });
669.       return;
670.     }
671. 
672.     const discordConfig = getDiscordConfig();
673.     if (!discordConfig.clientId || !discordConfig.clientSecret) {
674.       res.status(503).json({ error: 'Discord activity auth unavailable', code: 'NOT_CONFIGURED' });
675.       return;
676.     }
677. 
678.     const exchangeConfig: DiscordOAuthConfig = {
679.       ...discordConfig,
680.       redirectUri: redirectUriInput || discordConfig.redirectUri,
681.     };
682. 
683.     // Timeout fallback keeps this endpoint responsive if Discord is degraded.
684.     const exchangeResult = await Promise.race([
685.       exchangeDiscordCode(code, exchangeConfig),
686.       new Promise<{ success: false; error: string }>((resolve) => {
687.         setTimeout(() => resolve({ success: false, error: 'Discord token exchange timeout' }), 8000);
688.       }),
689.     ]);
690. 
691.     if (!exchangeResult.success || !exchangeResult.tokens) {
692.       res.status(401).json({ error: 'Discord token exchange failed', code: 'DISCORD_EXCHANGE_FAILED' });
693.       return;
694.     }
695. 
696.     res.json({
697.       access_token: exchangeResult.tokens.accessToken,
698.       token_type: exchangeResult.tokens.tokenType,
699.       expires_in: exchangeResult.tokens.expiresIn,
700.       scope: exchangeResult.tokens.scope,
701.     });
702.   } catch (error) {
703.     console.error('[Auth] Discord activity token exchange error:', error);
704.     res.status(500).json({ error: 'Activity authentication failed', code: 'ACTIVITY_AUTH_FAILED' });
705.   }
706. });
707. 
708. /**
709.  * GET /auth/me
710.  * Returns current user info from JWT token or session cookie
711.  */
712. router.get('/me', async (req, res) => {
713.   try {
714.     // Try JWT token first (from Authorization header)
715.     const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
716.     if (authHeader && authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
717.       const token = authHeader.split(' ')[1];
718.       const secret = getJWTSecret();
719. 
720.       try {
721.         const payload = jwt.verify(token, secret) as { userId: string; email: string; roles: string[] };
722.         const user = await findUserById(payload.userId);
723. 
724.         if (user) {
725.           res.json({
726.             userId: user.id,
727.             email: user.email,
728.             discordId: user.discord_id,
729.             discordUsername: user.discord_username,
730.             walletAddress: user.wallet_address,
731.             roles: user.roles,
732.             type: 'user',
733.             isAdmin: user.roles.includes('admin'),
734.           });
735.           return;
736.         }
737.       } catch (jwtError) {
738.         // Token invalid, try session cookie
739.       }
740.     }
741. 
742.     // Fallback to session cookie (Discord OAuth)
743.     const jwtConfig = getJWTConfig();
744.     const cookieHeader = req.headers.cookie;
745. 
746.     const result = await verifySessionCookie(cookieHeader, jwtConfig);
747. 
748.     if (!result.valid || !result.session) {
749.       res.status(401).json({ error: 'Not authenticated', code: 'UNAUTHORIZED' });
750.       return;
751.     }
752. 
753.     const session = result.session;
754. 
755.     res.json({
756.       userId: session.userId,
757.       type: session.type,
758.       discordId: session.discordId,
759.       discordUsername: session.discordUsername,
760.       walletAddress: session.walletAddress,
761.       roles: session.roles,
762.       isAdmin: session.type === 'admin',
763.     });
764.   } catch (error) {
765.     console.error('[Auth] Get me error:', error);
766.     res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get user info' });
767.   }
768. });
769. 
770. /**
771.  * POST /auth/logout
772.  * Destroys the current session
773.  */
774. router.post('/logout', (_req, res) => {
775.   try {
776.     const cookie = destroySession();
777.     res.setHeader('Set-Cookie', cookie);
778.     res.json({ success: true, message: 'Logged out successfully' });
779.   } catch (error) {
780.     console.error('[Auth] Logout error:', error);
781.     res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to logout' });
782.   }
783. });
784. 
785. /**
786.  * GET /auth/logout
787.  * Alternative logout via GET (for links)
788.  */
789. router.get('/logout', (_req, res) => {
790.   try {
791.     const cookie = destroySession();
792.     res.setHeader('Set-Cookie', cookie);
793.     res.redirect('https://tiltcheck.me');
794.   } catch (error) {
795.     console.error('[Auth] Logout error:', error);
796.     res.redirect('https://tiltcheck.me');
797.   }
798. });
799. 
800. export { router as authRouter };

30.   max: 10,
31.   standardHeaders: true,
32.   legacyHeaders: false,
33. });
34. const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? (() => { throw new Error('JWT_SECRET is required in production'); })() : 'tiltcheck-user-secret-2024');
35. const magicAdmin = new Magic(process.env.MAGIC_SECRET_KEY);
36. const solanaConnection = new Connection(process.env.SOLANA_RPC_URL || 'https://api.mainnet-beta.solana.com', 'confirmed');
37. 
38. // Middleware
39. app.use(cors());
40. app.use(express.json());
41. app.use(express.static(join(__dirname, '../public')));
42. 
43. // === Types ===
44. interface UserData {
45.   discordId: string;
46.   username: string;
47.   avatar: string;
48.   trustScore: number;
49.   tiltLevel: number;
50.   analytics?: {
51.     totalJuice: number;
52.     totalTipsCaught: number;
53.     eventCount: number;
54.     wagered: number;
55.     deposited: number;
56.     profit: number;
57.   };
58.   degenIdentity?: DegenIdentity | null;
59.   recentActivity: ActivityItem[];
60.   preferences: UserPreferences;
61. }
62. 
63. interface ActivityItem {
64.   type: string;
65.   description: string;
66.   timestamp: number;
67. }
68. 
69. interface UserPreferences {
70.   notifyBonus: boolean;
71.   notifyJuice: boolean;
72. 
73.   anonTipping: boolean;
74.   showAnalytics: boolean;
75.   baseCurrency: string;
76. }
77. 
78. interface DiscordUser {
79.   discordId: string;
80.   username: string;
81. }
82. 
83. interface AuthenticatedRequest extends Request {
84.   user?: DiscordUser;
85. }
86. 
87. // === Data Fetching ===
88. async function getUserData(discordId: string): Promise<UserData | null> {
89.   if (!db.isConnected()) return null;
90. 
91.   try {
92.     const [dbStats, dbPrefs, dbIdentity] = await Promise.all([
93.       db.getUserStats(discordId),
94.       db.getUserPreferences(discordId),
95.       db.getDegenIdentity(discordId)
96.     ]);
97. 
98.     if (!dbStats) return null;
99. 
100.     return {
101.       discordId: dbStats.discord_id,
102.       username: dbStats.username,
103.       avatar: dbStats.avatar || '',
104.       trustScore: dbIdentity?.trust_score ?? 50,
105.       tiltLevel: 0,
106.       analytics: {
107.         totalJuice: 0, // Future: Pull from distribution table
108.         totalTipsCaught: 0,
109.         eventCount: 0,
110.         wagered: Number(dbStats.wagered_amount_sol),
111.         deposited: Number(dbStats.deposited_amount_sol),
112.         profit: Number(dbStats.profit_sol)
113.       },
114.       degenIdentity: dbIdentity,
115.       recentActivity: [],
116.       preferences: {
117.         notifyBonus: true,
118.         notifyJuice: true,
119.         anonTipping: false,
120.         showAnalytics: true,
121.         baseCurrency: 'SOL'
122.       }
123.     };
124.   } catch (err) {
125.     return null;
126.   }
127. }
128. 
129. // === Auth Routes ===
130. const DISCORD_CONFIG = {
131.   clientId: process.env.DISCORD_CLIENT_ID,
132.   clientSecret: process.env.DISCORD_CLIENT_SECRET,
133.   redirectUri: process.env.DISCORD_CALLBACK_URL || 'http://localhost:6001/auth/discord/callback'
134. };
135. 
136. app.get('/auth/discord', (_req, res) => {
137.   const url = `https://discord.com/api/oauth2/authorize?client_id=${DISCORD_CONFIG.clientId}&redirect_uri=${encodeURIComponent(DISCORD_CONFIG.redirectUri)}&response_type=code&scope=identify%20email`;
138.   res.redirect(url);
139. });
140. 
141. app.get('/auth/discord/callback', async (req, res) => {
142.   const { code } = req.query;
143.   if (!code) return res.redirect('/?error=no_code');
144. 
145.   try {
146.     const tokenRes = await fetch('https://discord.com/api/oauth2/token', {
147.       method: 'POST',
148.       headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' },
149.       body: new URLSearchParams({
150.         client_id: DISCORD_CONFIG.clientId!,
151.         client_secret: DISCORD_CONFIG.clientSecret!,
152.         grant_type: 'authorization_code',
153.         code: code as string,
154.         redirect_uri: DISCORD_CONFIG.redirectUri,
155.       }),
156.     });
157. 
158.     const { access_token } = await tokenRes.json() as any;
159.     const userRes = await fetch('https://discord.com/api/users/@me', {
160.       headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${access_token}` },
161.     });
162. 
163.     const userData = await userRes.json() as any;
164.     const token = jwt.sign(
165.       { discordId: userData.id, username: userData.username, avatar: userData.avatar },
166.       JWT_SECRET,
167.       { expiresIn: '7d' }
168.     );
169. 
170.     res.redirect(`/dashboard?token=${token}`);
171.   } catch (err) {
172.     res.redirect('/?error=auth_failed');
173.   }
174. });
175. 
176. // === API Routes ===
177. app.get('/api/auth/me', authenticateToken as any, (req: any, res) => {
178.   res.json(req.user);
179. });
180. 
181. app.get('/api/user/:discordId', authenticateToken as any, async (req: any, res) => {
182.   const data = await getUserData(req.params.discordId);
183.   if (!data) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'User not found' });
184.   res.json(data);
185. });
186. 
187. app.get('/api/user/:discordId/trust', authenticateToken as any, trustLimiter, async (req: any, res) => {
188.   const data = await getUserData(req.params.discordId);
189.   if (!data) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'User not found' });
190.   
191.   res.json({
192.     trustScore: data.trustScore,
193.     tiltLevel: data.tiltLevel,
194.     factors: { consistency: 85, community: 70 }
195.   });
196. });
197. 
198. app.get('/api/user/:discordId/activity', authenticateToken as any, async (req: any, res) => {
199.   // Mock activity for now
200.   res.json({
201.     activities: [
202.       { type: 'juice', description: 'Caught 0.05 SOL in /juice drop', timestamp: Date.now() - 3600000 },
203.       { type: 'tip', description: 'Received 0.1 SOL tip from @DegenMaster', timestamp: Date.now() - 86400000 }
204.     ]
205.   });
206. });
207. 
208. app.put('/api/user/:discordId/preferences', authenticateToken as any, async (req: any, res) => {
209.   // Logic to save preferences to DB
210.   res.json({ success: true });
211. });
212. 
213. app.post('/api/auth/wallet/link', authenticateToken as any, async (req: any, res) => {
214.   const { address, signature, message } = req.body;
215.   // Verify signature and save to DB
216.   if (db.isConnected()) {
217.     await db.upsertDegenIdentity({
218.       discord_id: req.user!.discordId,
219.       primary_external_address: address
220.     });
221.   }
222.   res.json({ success: true });
223. });
224. 
225. app.post('/api/auth/magic/link', authenticateToken as any, async (req: any, res) => {
226.   const { didToken } = req.body;
227.   const metadata = await magicAdmin.users.getMetadataByToken(didToken);
228.   if (db.isConnected()) {
229.     await db.upsertDegenIdentity({
230.       discord_id: req.user!.discordId,
231.       magic_address: metadata.publicAddress
232.     });
233.   }
234.   res.json({ success: true, address: metadata.publicAddress });
235. });
236. 
237. // === AI Agent Route ===
238. app.post('/api/agent/query', authenticateToken as any, async (req: any, res) => {
239.   const { query } = req.body;
240.   if (!query) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing query' });
241. 
242.   try {
243.     let finalResponse = '';
244.     const it = runner.runAsync({
245.       userId: req.user.discordId,
246.       sessionId: 'dashboard-session',
247.       newMessage: {
248.         role: 'user',
249.         parts: [{ text: query }]
250.       }
251.     });
252. 
253.     for await (const event of it) {
254.       finalResponse = stringifyContent(event);
255.     }
256. 
257.     res.json({ response: finalResponse });
258.   } catch (err) {
259.     console.error('[Agent] Error:', err);
260.     res.status(500).json({ error: 'Agent failed to process query' });
261.   }
262. });
263. 
264. // === Middleware ===
265. function authenticateToken(req: AuthenticatedRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) {
266.   const authHeader = req.headers['authorization'];
267.   const token = authHeader && authHeader.split(' ')[1];
268.   if (!token) return res.sendStatus(401);
269. 
270.   jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET, (err: any, user: any) => {
271.     if (err) return res.sendStatus(403);
272.     req.user = user;
273.     next();
274.   });
275. }
276. 
277. app.get('/dashboard', (_req, res) => {
278.   res.sendFile(join(__dirname, '../public/index.html'));
279. });
280. 
281. const isMainModule = process.argv[1] && import.meta.url === pathToFileURL(process.argv[1]).href;
282. if (isMainModule) {
283.   app.listen(PORT, () => {
284.     console.log(`рҹҺҜ Degen Hub listening on port ${PORT}`);
285.   });
286. }
287. 
288. export { app };
```

1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. /**
3.  * MV3 service worker.
4.  * Sidebar-first controls and shared tab actions.
5.  */
6. 
7. const VAULT_URL_BASE = 'https://tiltcheck.me/vault';
8. const ALLOWED_AUTH_ORIGINS = new Set(['https://api.tiltcheck.me', 'http://localhost', 'http://127.0.0.1']);
9. 
10. function isAllowedAuthUrl(value) {
11.   try {
12.     const parsed = new URL(value);
13.     if (!ALLOWED_AUTH_ORIGINS.has(parsed.origin)) return false;
14.     return parsed.pathname === '/auth/discord/login';
15.   } catch {
16.     return false;
17.   }
18. }
19. 
20. chrome.runtime.onInstalled.addListener(() => {
21.   console.log('[TiltCheck] Extension installed');
22. });
23. 
24. chrome.action.onClicked.addListener((tab) => {
25.   if (!tab?.id) return;
26. 
27.   chrome.tabs.sendMessage(tab.id, { type: 'toggle_sidebar' }, () => {
28.     if (chrome.runtime.lastError) {
29.       console.log('[TiltCheck] Sidebar unavailable on this tab:', chrome.runtime.lastError.message);
30.     }
31.   });
32. });
33. 
34. function buildVaultUrl(suggestedAmount) {
35.   const amount = Number(suggestedAmount);
36.   if (Number.isFinite(amount) && amount > 0) {
37.     return `${VAULT_URL_BASE}?amount=${amount}`;
38.   }
39.   return VAULT_URL_BASE;
40. }
41. 
42. // Handle extension-wide actions requested from content scripts.
43. chrome.runtime.onMessage.addListener((message, sender, sendResponse) => {
44.   if (message.type === 'open_auth_bridge') {
45.     const authUrl = typeof message.url === 'string' ? message.url : null;
46.     if (!authUrl || !isAllowedAuthUrl(authUrl)) {
47.       sendResponse({ success: false, error: 'Invalid auth URL' });
48.       return false;
49.     }
50.     const bridgeUrl = chrome.runtime.getURL(`auth-bridge.html?authUrl=${encodeURIComponent(authUrl)}`);
51.     const createOptions = { url: bridgeUrl, active: true };
52.     if (typeof sender?.tab?.windowId === 'number') {
53.       createOptions.windowId = sender.tab.windowId;
54.       if (typeof sender.tab.index === 'number') {
55.         createOptions.index = sender.tab.index + 1;
56.       }
57.     }
58.     chrome.tabs.create(createOptions, () => {
59.       if (chrome.runtime.lastError) {
60.         sendResponse({ success: false, error: chrome.runtime.lastError.message });
61.         return;
62.       }
63.       sendResponse({ success: true });
64.     });
65.     return true;
66.   }
67. 
68.   if (message.type === 'open_auth_tab') {
69.     const url = typeof message.url === 'string' ? message.url : null;
70.     if (!url) {
71.       sendResponse({ success: false, error: 'Missing auth URL' });
72.       return false;
73.     }
74.     const createOptions = { url, active: true };
75.     if (typeof sender?.tab?.windowId === 'number') {
76.       createOptions.windowId = sender.tab.windowId;
77.       if (typeof sender.tab.index === 'number') {
78.         createOptions.index = sender.tab.index + 1;
79.       }
80.     }
81.     chrome.tabs.create(createOptions, () => {
82.       if (chrome.runtime.lastError) {
83.         sendResponse({ success: false, error: chrome.runtime.lastError.message });
84.         return;
85.       }
86.       sendResponse({ success: true });
87.     });
88.     return true;
89.   }
90. 
91.   if (message.type === 'open_vault') {
92.     const url = buildVaultUrl(message.data?.suggestedAmount);
93.     chrome.tabs.create({ url });
94.     sendResponse({ success: true });
95.     return false;
96.   }
97. 
98.   return false;
99. });
100.
```

214.     return {
215.       success: true,
216.       locked: lock.status === 'locked' || lock.status === 'extended',
217.       status: lock.status,
218.       amount: lock.lockedAmountSOL,
219.       amountUnit: 'SOL',
220.       unlockTime: new Date(lock.unlockAt).toISOString(),
221.       createdAt: new Date(lock.createdAt).toISOString(),
222.       id: lock.id,
223.       readyToRelease: now >= lock.unlockAt,
224.     };
225.   }
226. 
227.   const vaultMatch = endpoint.match(/^\/vault\/[^/]+$/);
228.   if (vaultMatch) {
229.     return {
230.       success: true,
231.       vault: {
232.         balance: Number(demoVaultBalance.toFixed(2)),
233.         locks: getDemoLocks(),
234.       },
235.     };
236.   }
237. 
238.   return { success: true, demo: true };
239. }
240. 
241. function escapeHtml(value: unknown): string {
242.   return String(value ?? '')
243.     .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
244.     .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
245.     .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
246.     .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
247.     .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
248. }
249. 
250. function getStorage(keys: string[] | string): Promise<Record<string, any>> {
251.   return new Promise((resolve) => {
252.     try {
253.       if (!chrome.runtime?.id) {
254.         console.warn('[TiltCheck] Extension context invalidated. Please refresh the page.');
255.         resolve({});
256.         return;
257.       }
258.       chrome.storage.local.get(keys, (result) => {
259.         if (chrome.runtime?.lastError) {
260.           console.warn('[TiltCheck] Storage get failed:', chrome.runtime.lastError.message);
261.           resolve({});
262.           return;
263.         }
264.         resolve(result || {});
265.       });
266.     } catch (error) {
267.       console.warn('[TiltCheck] Storage get exception:', error);
268.       resolve({});
269.     }
270.   });
271. }
272. 
273. function setStorage(values: Record<string, any>): Promise<void> {
274.   return new Promise((resolve) => {
275.     try {
276.       chrome.storage.local.set(values, () => resolve());
277.     } catch (error) {
278.       console.warn('[TiltCheck] Storage set exception:', error);
279.       resolve();
280.     }
281.   });
282. }
283. 
284. function removeStorage(keys: string[] | string): Promise<void> {
285.   return new Promise((resolve) => {
286.     try {
287.       chrome.storage.local.remove(keys, () => resolve());
288.     } catch (error) {
289.       console.warn('[TiltCheck] Storage remove exception:', error);
290.       resolve();
291.     }
292.   });
293. }
294. 
295. function formatLockRemaining(ms: number): string {
296.   const totalSec = Math.max(0, Math.ceil(ms / 1000));
297.   const hrs = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600);
298.   const mins = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
299.   const sec = totalSec % 60;
300.   if (hrs > 0) return `${hrs}h ${mins}m ${sec}s`;
301.   return `${mins}m ${sec}s`;
302. }
303. 
304. async function ensureWalletUnlocked(actionLabel: string): Promise<boolean> {
305.   if (!userData || demoMode) return true;
306.   const state = await apiCall(`/vault/${userData.id}/lock-status`);
307.   const isLocked = state?.locked === true;
308.   if (isLocked) {
309.     const remainingMs = Number(state?.remainingMs)
310.       || Math.max(0, new Date(String(state?.unlockTime || 0)).getTime() - Date.now());
311.     const remaining = formatLockRemaining(remainingMs);
312.     const message = `Wallet lock is active (${remaining}). Unlock in sidebar to ${actionLabel}.`;
313.     updateStatus(message, 'warning');
314.     addFeedMessage(message);
315.     return false;
316.   }
317.   return true;
318. }
319. 
320. function applyPageOffset(width: number) {
321.   const offset = `${width}px`;
322. 
323.   // Some sites anchor layout to <html>, others to <body>. Set both so content shifts reliably.
324.   document.documentElement.style.marginRight = offset;
325.   document.documentElement.style.transition = 'margin-right 0.3s ease';
326.   document.body.style.marginRight = offset;
327.   document.body.style.transition = 'margin-right 0.3s ease';
328. }
329. 
330. function setSidebarVisibility(visible: boolean) {
331.   const sidebar = document.getElementById('tiltcheck-sidebar');
332.   if (!sidebar) return;
333.   sidebar.style.display = visible ? 'block' : 'none';
334.   try {
335.     chrome.storage.local.set({ [SIDEBAR_VISIBILITY_KEY]: visible });
336.   } catch {
337.     // Ignore storage failures in restricted contexts.
338.   }
339.   if (!visible) {
340.     applyPageOffset(0);
341.     return;
342.   }
343.   const width = sidebar.classList.contains('minimized') ? MINIMIZED_WIDTH : SIDEBAR_WIDTH;
344.   applyPageOffset(width);
345. }
346. 
347. async function updateSidebarPrefs(partial: Record<string, any>) {
348.   const result = await getStorage([SIDEBAR_PREFS_KEY]);
349.   const existing = result[SIDEBAR_PREFS_KEY] || {};
350.   await setStorage({ [SIDEBAR_PREFS_KEY]: { ...existing, ...partial } });
```

353. function setSidebarMinimized(minimized: boolean, persist = true) {

395. async function restoreSidebarPreferences() {
396.   const result = await getStorage([SIDEBAR_PREFS_KEY]);
397.   const prefs = result[SIDEBAR_PREFS_KEY];
398.   if (typeof prefs?.minimized === 'boolean') {
399.     setSidebarMinimized(prefs.minimized, false);
400.   }
401.   if (typeof prefs?.showAdvanced === 'boolean') {
402.     setAdvancedToolsVisibility(prefs.showAdvanced, false);
403.   } else {
404.     setAdvancedToolsVisibility(false, false);
405.   }

408. async function apiCall(endpoint: string, options: any = {}) {
409.   if (demoMode) {
410.     return mockApiCall(endpoint, options);
411.   }
412.   const headers: any = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
413.   if (authToken) headers['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${authToken}`;
414. 
415.   try {
416.     const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}${endpoint}`, {
417.       ...options,
418.       headers: { ...headers, ...options.headers }
419.     });
420.     return await response.json();
421.   } catch (error) {
422.     console.error('API Error:', error);
423.     return { error: 'Network issue. Try again.' };
424.   }
425. }

441. /**
442.  * Call backend AI service for intelligent analysis
443.  */
444. async function callAIGateway(application: string, data: any = {}) {
445.   try {
446.     const response = await fetch(`${AI_GATEWAY_URL}/api/ai`, {
447.       method: 'POST',
448.       headers: {
449.         'Content-Type': 'application/json',
450.         ...(authToken ? { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${authToken}` } : {})
451.       },
452.       body: JSON.stringify({
453.         application,
454.         prompt: data.prompt || '',
455.         context: data.context || {}
456.       })
457.     });
458. 
459.     if (response.ok) {
460.       return await response.json();
461.     }
462.     console.log('[TiltCheck] Backend AI request failed, using local fallback');
463.     return { success: false, error: 'Request did not complete. Try again.' };
464.   } catch (error) {
465.     console.log('[TiltCheck] Backend AI offline, using local fallback');
466.     return { success: false, error: 'Network issue. Try again.' };
467.   }
468. }

1406. function clearDiscordAuthPolling() {
1407.   if (discordAuthPollIntervalId) {
1408.     clearInterval(discordAuthPollIntervalId);
1409.     discordAuthPollIntervalId = null;
1410.   }
1411. }
1412. 
1413. async function applyDiscordAuthSuccess(token: string, user: Record<string, any>) {
1414.   await setStorage({ authToken: token, userData: user });
1415.   clearDiscordAuthPolling();
1416.   demoMode = false;
1417.   authToken = token;
1418.   userData = { ...user, isDemo: false };
1419.   isAuthenticated = true;
1420.   showMainContent();
1421.   syncAccountUi();
1422.   addFeedMessage(`Connected: ${userData.username || 'TiltCheck user'}`);
1423. }
1424. 
1425. function handleDiscordAuthMessage(event: MessageEvent) {
1426.   if (event.origin !== API_ORIGIN) return;
1427.   const data = event.data as { type?: string; token?: unknown; user?: unknown } | null;
1428.   if (!data || data.type !== DISCORD_AUTH_MESSAGE_TYPE) return;
1429.   if (typeof data.token !== 'string' || !data.token) return;
1430.   if (!data.user || typeof data.user !== 'object') return;
1431.   void applyDiscordAuthSuccess(data.token, data.user as Record<string, any>);
1432. }
1433. 
1434. function startDiscordLoginFlow() {
1435.   const authUrl = getDiscordLoginUrl('extension');
1436.   const maxPollMs = 5 * 60 * 1000;
1437.   const startedAt = Date.now();
1438.   clearDiscordAuthPolling();
1439. 
1440.   const startStoragePolling = () => {
1441.     discordAuthPollIntervalId = setInterval(async () => {
1442.       try {
1443.         const stored = await getStorage(['authToken', 'userData']);
1444.         if (stored?.authToken && stored?.userData) {
1445.           await applyDiscordAuthSuccess(stored.authToken, stored.userData);
1446.           return;
1447.         }
1448. 
1449.         if (Date.now() - startedAt > maxPollMs) {
1450.           clearDiscordAuthPolling();
1451.           addFeedMessage('Discord connect timed out. Try again.');
1452.         }
1453.       } catch (error) {
1454.         clearDiscordAuthPolling();
1455.         console.warn('[TiltCheck] Discord connect polling failed:', error);
1456.         addFeedMessage('Discord connect interrupted. Reload the tab and try again.');
1457.       }
1458.     }, 1000);
1459.   };
1460. 
1461.   try {
1462.     // User-clicked popup preserves window.opener for callback postMessage.
1463.     const popup = window.open(authUrl, '_blank', 'popup=yes,width=520,height=760');
1464.     if (popup) {
1465.       startStoragePolling();
1466.       return;
1467.     }
1468. 
1469.     chrome.runtime.sendMessage({ type: 'open_auth_bridge', url: authUrl }, (response) => {
1470.       if (chrome.runtime.lastError) {
1471.         const msg = chrome.runtime.lastError.message || 'Could not open Discord login tab.';
1472.         addFeedMessage(
1473.           msg.includes('Extension context invalidated')
1474.             ? 'Extension refreshed mid-login. Reload this tab and retry Connect Discord.'
1475.             : 'Could not open Discord login helper. Try again.'
1476.         );
1477.         return;
1478.       }
1479. 
1480.       if (!response?.success) {
1481.         addFeedMessage('Could not open Discord login helper. Try again.');
1482.         return;
1483.       }
1484. 
1485.       addFeedMessage('Opened Discord login helper tab.');
1486.       startStoragePolling();
1487.     });
1488.   } catch (error) {
1489.     console.warn('[TiltCheck] Unable to start Discord connect flow:', error);
1490.     addFeedMessage('Connect failed to start. Reload tab and try again.');
1491.   }
1492. }
1493.

1497.

1517.       panel.style.display = showSettings ? 'block' : 'none';
1518.     }
1519.   });
1520.

1522.     const panel = document.getElementById('tg-settings-panel');
1523.     if (panel) {
1524.       showSettings = false;
1525.       panel.style.display = 'none';
1526.     }

1530.   const buddyCheckbox = document.getElementById('cfg-buddy-mirror') as HTMLInputElement;
1531.   if (buddyCheckbox) {
1532.     let buddyMirrorTouched = false;
1533.     buddyCheckbox.checked = buddyMirrorEnabled;
1534. 
1535.     void (async () => {
1536.       const settings = await getStorage(['buddyMirrorEnabled']);
1537.       if (typeof settings.buddyMirrorEnabled === 'boolean') {
1538.         buddyMirrorEnabled = settings.buddyMirrorEnabled;
1539.       } else {
1540.         // One-time migration from localStorage legacy key.
1541.         const legacyMirror = localStorage.getItem('tiltcheck_buddy_mirror');
1542.         if (legacyMirror !== null) {
1543.           buddyMirrorEnabled = legacyMirror === 'true';
1544.           await setStorage({ buddyMirrorEnabled });
1545.           localStorage.removeItem('tiltcheck_buddy_mirror');
1546.         }
1547.       }
1548.       // Avoid clobbering a user toggle that happened before async hydration finished.
1549.       if (!buddyMirrorTouched) {
1550.         buddyCheckbox.checked = buddyMirrorEnabled;
1551.       }
1552.     })();
1553. 
1554.     buddyCheckbox.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
1555.       buddyMirrorTouched = true;
1556.       buddyMirrorEnabled = (e.target as HTMLInputElement).checked;
1557.       void setStorage({ buddyMirrorEnabled });
1558.     });
1559.   }
1560. 
1561.   // Configurator toggle

1563.     const panel = document.getElementById('tg-config-panel');
1564.     if (panel) panel.style.display = 'block';
1565.   });

### рҹ’¬ Copilot

Perfect! Now I have enough information to provide a comprehensive analysis. Let me create the structured report:

## Discord OAuth Implementation Analysis - TiltCheck Monorepo

### Executive Summary
I've identified **critical mismatches and design issues** between the web and extension OAuth implementations that could cause login failures. The primary issues stem from **state validation fallback logic**, **cookie domain misconfigurations**, and **storage race conditions** in the extension flow.

---

## 1. OAuth Configuration

### Current Setup
**Location:** `packages/auth/src/discord.ts` and `apps/api/src/routes/auth.ts`

| Component | Configuration |
|-----------|---|
| **Client ID** | `1445916179163250860` (from `apps/chrome-extension/src/config.ts`) |
| **Redirect URI** | `https://api.tiltcheck.me/auth/discord/callback` |
| **Scopes** | `['identify', 'identify.premium']` |
| **State Generation** | `generateOAuthState()` - Cryptographically random 64-char hex string |

**Extension Config File:** `apps/chrome-extension/src/config.ts`
```typescript
DISCORD_REDIRECT_URI: 'https://api.tiltcheck.me/auth/discord/callback'
```

---

## 2. Web App OAuth Flow

### Location: `apps/api/src/routes/auth.ts` & `apps/user-dashboard/src/index.ts`

#### API-Based Flow (Recommended)
1. **GET `/auth/discord/login`** (lines 392-473)
   - Generates state with `ext_` or `web_` prefix
   - Stores state in `oauth_state` cookie (httpOnly, 10 min expiry)
   - Stores source in `oauth_source` cookie
   - Stores optional redirect URL in `oauth_redirect` cookie
   - Redirects to Discord authorization URL

2. **GET `/auth/discord/callback`** (lines 479-645)
   - Validates state against cookie
   - **FALLBACK FOR LOCAL DEV:** If state missing, allows extension callback if state prefix is `ext_` (lines 504-506)
   - Exchanges code for tokens
   - Creates user in DB
   - Sets session cookie with JWT
   - Returns `Set-Cookie` header with session token

#### Dashboard Service Flow (Legacy)
**Location:** `apps/user-dashboard/src/index.ts` (lines 136-174)
- **ISSUE:** No state validation!
- Simply exchanges code and redirects with token in URL query string (line 170)
- Token exposed in browser history and referer headers

---

## 3. Chrome Extension OAuth Flow

### Location: `apps/chrome-extension/src/`

#### Three-Step Flow:

**Step 1: Extension Initiates Login** (`sidebar.ts:1434-1492`)
```typescript
function startDiscordLoginFlow() {
  const authUrl = getDiscordLoginUrl('extension');  // gets /auth/discord/login?source=extension
  
  // Attempt 1: Direct popup
  const popup = window.open(authUrl, '_blank', 'popup=yes,width=520,height=760');
  if (popup) {
    startStoragePolling();  // Poll chrome.storage.local for authToken
    return;
  }
  
  // Attempt 2: Service worker bridge
  chrome.runtime.sendMessage({ type: 'open_auth_bridge', url: authUrl }, ...);
}
```

**Step 2: Auth Bridge Tab** (`auth-bridge.html` & `auth-bridge.js`)
- Opens auth popup from extension context
- Listens for `discord-auth` message from callback page
- Stores result in `chrome.storage.local`:
  ```javascript
  chrome.storage.local.set({
    authToken: data.token,
    userData: data.user,
  }, ...)
  ```

**Step 3: Callback to Auth Bridge**
`apps/api/src/routes/auth.ts:570-628` - **CRITICAL LOGIC:**
```typescript
if (source === 'extension') {
  if (!postMessageTarget) {  // Missing trusted origin
    return renderExtensionAuthErrorPage('Missing trusted extension origin...');
  }
  
  // Generate JWT and post to opener
  window.opener.postMessage({
    type: 'discord-auth',
    token: JWT,
    user: { id, username, avatar }
  }, postMessageTarget);  // postMessageTarget is extension origin
}
```

---

## 4. API Endpoints Summary

| Endpoint | Method | Purpose | Key Logic |
|----------|--------|---------|-----------|
| `/auth/discord/login` | GET | Initiate OAuth | Generates state with prefix, stores cookies |
| `/auth/discord/callback` | GET | Handle Discord redirect | Validates state, creates session |
| `/auth/discord/activity/token` | POST | Activity OAuth | Exchange code for tokens |
| `/auth/me` | GET | Get user info | JWT or cookie-based auth |
| `/auth/logout` | POST/GET | Destroy session | Clears cookies |

---

## 5. State Validation - Critical Issues

### Location: `apps/api/src/routes/auth.ts:501-511`

```typescript
const stateValid =
  !!stateValue &&
  (stateValue === storedState || 
   (!storedState && isLocalDev && sourceFromState === 'extension'));
```

### **ISSUES IDENTIFIED:**

#### Issue #1: Cookie Domain Mismatch
- **Web Cookie Domain:** `.tiltcheck.me` (from `packages/auth/src/cookies.ts:22`)
- **Extension Context:** Chrome extension can't access cookies set for `.tiltcheck.me` domain
- **Symptom:** State validation fails because `req.cookies.oauth_state` is undefined in extension flow
- **Fallback:** Only works in **local dev** when `isLocalDev && sourceFromState === 'extension'`

#### Issue #2: State Prefix Dependency
The code relies on state prefix to recover source when cookies are missing:
```typescript
const sourceFromState = stateValue.startsWith('ext_') ? 'extension' : 
                        stateValue.startsWith('web_') ? 'web' : undefined;
```
- **Problem:** In production, if cookies fail to be sent to API, state validation depends entirely on this prefix
- **No CSRF protection** if state can be guessed/reused

#### Issue #3: Local Dev Fallback Too Permissive
- Production: **REQUIRES** state to match cookie value (stricter)
- Development: Allows extension callback to succeed with just prefix match (looser)
- Could hide production bugs during testing

#### Issue #4: Source Validation is Secondary
```typescript
if (sourceFromCookie && sourceFromState && sourceFromCookie !== sourceFromState) {
  res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid OAuth source' });
  return;
}
```
- Only validates if **both** exist
- If either is missing, validation is skipped
- In extension flow, cookie is likely missing вҶ’ validation skipped

---

## 6. Cookie/Redirect Handling Issues

### Web App Cookies
**Set by:** `apps/api/src/routes/auth.ts:428-453`

```typescript
res.cookie('oauth_state', state, {
  httpOnly: true,
  secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
  sameSite: 'lax',
  maxAge: 10 * 60 * 1000,  // 10 minutes
});
```

**Issues:**
1. **Missing `domain` parameter** - Will use host only, not shared domain
2. **sameSite: lax** - Will send cross-site cookies with user-initiated requests (OK for redirects, but vulnerable)
3. **No `path` parameter** - Defaults to request path, may not be `/`

### Extension Storage (Not HTTP Cookies)
**Location:** `apps/chrome-extension/src/auth-bridge.js:59-78`

```typescript
chrome.storage.local.set(
  {
    authToken: data.token,
    userData: data.user,
  },
  () =\> { /* callback */ }
);
```

**Issues:**
1. **No error handling** for storage quota exceeded
2. **No retry logic** if storage write fails
3. **No timeout** on storage operations
4. **Race condition:** If sidebar polling reads before bridge writes, auth fails silently

---

## 7. Cross-Origin & Header Issues

### postMessage Validation
**Location:** `apps/api/src/routes/auth.ts:568-625`

```typescript
const postMessageTarget = getTrustedExtensionOrigin(openerOriginCookie);
if (!postMessageTarget) {
  return renderExtensionAuthErrorPage('Missing trusted extension origin...');
}

window.opener.postMessage({
  type: 'discord-auth',
  token: token,
  user: userData
}, postMessageTarget);
```

**Issues:**
1. **Extension runtime ID required** - `chrome-extension://\<runtime-id\>`
2. **Runtime ID changes per installation** - Changes when extension is reinstalled
3. **No timeout** on postMessage - If window closed, message sent to void
4. **No acknowledgment** - No way to verify message was received

### Extension Origin Verification
**Location:** `apps/chrome-extension/src/auth-bridge.js:9`

```typescript
const allowedOrigins = new Set(['https://api.tiltcheck.me', 'http://localhost', 'http://127.0.0.1']);
const apiOrigin = (() =\> {
  const origin = new URL(authUrl || 'https://api.tiltcheck.me').origin;
  return allowedOrigins.has(origin) ? origin : 'https://api.tiltcheck.me';
})();
```

**Issue:** Trusts origin from query parameter - no validation that it came from trusted callback

---

## 8. Recent Git Issues - Merge Conflict

**Location:** `apps/api/tests/routes/auth-oauth-state.test.ts:36-41`

```typescript
\<\<\<\<\<\<\< HEAD
import { createSession, exchangeDiscordCode, verifyDiscordOAuth } from '@tiltcheck/auth';
import { findOrCreateUserByDiscord } from '@tiltcheck/db';
=======
import { exchangeDiscordCode } from '@tiltcheck/auth';
\>\>\>\>\>\>\> origin/main
```

**Issue:** Unresolved merge conflict in test file - test suite won't compile/run properly

---

## 9. User-Dashboard Legacy Implementation Issues

**Location:** `apps/user-dashboard/src/index.ts:141-174`

**Critical Problems:**
1. **NO STATE VALIDATION** - Exchanges code without validating OAuth state
2. **Token in URL** - Line 170: `res.redirect(\`/dashboard?token=${token}\`)`
   - Token visible in browser history
   - Leaked via Referer header to third-party domains
   - Stored in browser logs
3. **Different DISCORD_CONFIG** - Uses separate credentials:
   ```typescript
   const DISCORD_CONFIG = {
     clientId: process.env.DISCORD_CLIENT_ID,
     clientSecret: process.env.DISCORD_CLIENT_SECRET,
     redirectUri: process.env.DISCORD_CALLBACK_URL || 'http://localhost:6001/auth/discord/callback'
   };
   ```
4. **No JWT secret validation** - Could throw if JWT_SECRET not set

---

## 10. Summary Table: Web vs Extension Implementation

| Aspect | Web (apps/api) | Extension |
|--------|---|---|
| **State Validation** | Strict (must match cookie) | Fallback to prefix match in dev |
| **Storage Type** | HTTP Cookies | chrome.storage.local |
| **Cookie Domain** | .tiltcheck.me | N/A (not applicable) |
| **Message Passing** | HTTP redirects | postMessage + storage polling |
| **Token Location** | Secure cookie | chrome.storage.local |
| **CSRF Protection** | State cookie + prefix | State prefix only |
| **Error Handling** | HTTP errors | Silent failures |

---

## 11. Identified Login Problems

### **Problem 1: Production State Validation Failure**
- **Symptom:** Extension login fails in production with "Invalid OAuth state"
- **Root Cause:** 
  - Cookies set with `domain: .tiltcheck.me` not accessible from API backend cookie parser
  - Local dev fallback bypassed in production
  - State must match stored cookie value, but cookie never sent
- **Affected Flow:** Extension OAuth in production

### **Problem 2: Token Exposure in User Dashboard**
- **Symptom:** Auth tokens visible in browser history and logs
- **Root Cause:** JWT passed as URL query parameter in redirect
- **Affected Flow:** User dashboard OAuth callback
- **Severity:** HIGH - Token can be extracted from logs

### **Problem 3: Extension Storage Race Condition**
- **Symptom:** Sporadic "connect timed out" errors even on successful Discord auth
- **Root Cause:**
  - Bridge writes to storage asynchronously
  - Sidebar polls every 1000ms
  - Bridge auto-closes after 1200ms before write completes
  - If polling starts before write finishes, auth fails
- **Affected Flow:** Extension OAuth via auth-bridge
- **Location:** `sidebar.ts:1441-1458` polling vs `auth-bridge.js:76` close timeout

### **Problem 4: Missing Extension Origin Validation**
- **Symptom:** "Missing trusted extension origin" error even though extension is installed
- **Root Cause:**
  - Extension runtime ID not passed to login endpoint in all code paths
  - Runtime ID changes on reinstall
  - No fallback if runtime ID unavailable
- **Affected Flow:** Extension OAuth via auth-bridge
- **Location:** `config.ts:26-28` only sets if `chrome.runtime?.id` exists

### **Problem 5: No Error Recovery in User Dashboard**
- **Symptom:** Silent auth failures, users stuck on callback page
- **Root Cause:**
  - Errors caught but only redirect to `/?error=...` with no explanation
  - No retry mechanism
  - Token exchange timeout possible but not handled
- **Affected Flow:** User dashboard OAuth

### **Problem 6: Unresolved Merge Conflict in Tests**
- **Symptom:** Test suite won't run
- **Root Cause:** Merge conflict in `auth-oauth-state.test.ts` never resolved
- **Affected Flow:** All OAuth state validation testing

---

## 12. Recommendations (Priority)

| Priority | Issue | Solution |
|----------|-------|----------|
| **CRITICAL** | Extension state validation fails in production | Add domain parameter to oauth_state cookie: `domain: req.hostname` or remove domain for same-site only |
| **CRITICAL** | Token in URL in user-dashboard | Replace redirect with `Set-Cookie` header + POST redirect pattern |
| **CRITICAL** | Storage race condition in extension | Add `Promise.all([write, acknowledge])` instead of fire-and-forget |
| **HIGH** | Missing merge conflict resolution | Resolve git conflict in auth-oauth-state.test.ts |
| **HIGH** | No extension runtime ID validation | Pass runtime ID explicitly, store and validate on callback |
| **MEDIUM** | postMessage has no acknowledgment | Implement ACK message from extension back to callback page |
| **MEDIUM** | State validation too permissive | Remove local dev fallback or add explicit config flag |

---

| Component | Location |
|-----------|----------|
| OAuth Configuration | `packages/auth/src/discord.ts` |
| API Routes | `apps/api/src/routes/auth.ts` |
| Extension Config | `apps/chrome-extension/src/config.ts` |
| Extension Auth Bridge | `apps/chrome-extension/src/auth-bridge.{js,html}` |
| Extension Sidebar | `apps/chrome-extension/src/sidebar.ts` (lines 1413-1492) |
| Background Worker | `apps/chrome-extension/src/background.js` |
| Cookies Module | `packages/auth/src/cookies.ts` |
| User Dashboard | `apps/user-dashboard/src/index.ts` (lines 136-174) |
| Tests | `apps/api/tests/routes/auth-oauth-state.test.ts` |
