```
1. # TiltCheck Monorepo вҖ” Code Audit Report
2. 
3. > **Generated:** 2026-02-25 | **Scope:** Source code audit across apps/, modules/, packages/
4. 
5. ---
6. 
7. ## рҹҗӣ BUGS TO FIX (Code-Verified)
8. 
9. ### рҹ”ҙ Critical / High Priority
10. 
11. #### B1 вҖ” Chrome Extension: `manifest.json` is a PWA manifest, not a MV3 extension manifest
12. 
13. - **File:** `apps/chrome-extension/src/manifest.json`
14. - **Issue:** The file is a **Progressive Web App manifest** (has `start_url`, `display: standalone`, `orientation`). It is missing all required Chrome Extension MV3 fields: `manifest_version: 3`, `permissions`, `background.service_worker`, `content_scripts`, and `action`. The extension **will not load in Chrome as-is.**
15. - **Fix:** Replace with a proper MV3 manifest that declares `content_scripts: [content.js]`, `action` (popup), and required permissions (`storage`, `tabs`, `activeTab`).
16. 
17. #### B2 вҖ” Chrome Extension: `popup.html` references a non-existent `configBtn` / `configPanel`
18. 
19. - **File:** `apps/chrome-extension/src/popup.ts` (lines 66вҖ“68) vs `popup.html`
20. - **Issue:** `popup.ts` queries DOM elements `configBtn`, `configPanel`, `cfgCancel`, `cfgSave`, `cfgDomain`, `cfgBet`, `cfgResult` вҖ” **none of these exist in `popup.html`**. Every related event listener (`openConfigurator`, `saveConfiguration`, etc.) silently no-ops because the elements are null.
21. - **Fix:** Add the configurator panel/fields to `popup.html`, or remove the dead configurator code from `popup.ts`.
22. 
23. #### B3 вҖ” `report.ts` uses `DISCORD_TOKEN` as a server-to-server bearer token
24. 
25. - **File:** `apps/discord-bot/src/commands/report.ts` (line 57)
26. - **Issue:** `Authorization: Bearer ${process.env.DISCORD_TOKEN}` вҖ” the Discord bot token is **not** an API auth token and will be rejected by the backend. This means the `/report` command never actually persists anything.
27. - **Fix:** Use a dedicated `INTERNAL_API_SECRET` env var shared between the bot and API.
28. 
29. #### B4 вҖ” `handleAirdropClaim` is monkey-patched onto `tip` command with `as any`
30. 
31. - **File:** `apps/discord-bot/src/commands/tip.ts` (line 1472) / `events.ts` (line 166)
32. - **Issue:** `(tip as any).handleAirdropClaim = handleAirdropClaim;` and later `(tipCommand as any).handleAirdropClaim(...)`. This is a brittle workaround вҖ” no type safety, will silently fail if the property isn't set (e.g., if command load order changes).
33. - **Fix:** Create a shared button-handler registry (e.g., a `Map<string, ButtonHandler>`) and register airdrop claim there.
34. 
35. #### B5 вҖ” SusLink `followRedirects` passes an invalid `timeout` option to `fetch`
36. 
37. - **File:** `modules/suslink/src/scanner.ts` (line 247)
38. - **Issue:** `fetch(url, { ..., timeout: 5000, ... })` вҖ” the `timeout` property is **not a valid Fetch API option** in Node.js. It will be silently ignored, meaning redirect following never actually times out. Uses `as any` to suppress the TypeScript error.
39. - **Fix:** Use `AbortController` + `AbortSignal.timeout(5000)` as already done correctly in `modules/stake/src/client.ts`.
40. 
41. #### B6 вҖ” `walletcheck` module only scans ETH, but bot description says "EVM" without USDC support
42. 
43. - **File:** `modules/walletcheck/src/index.ts` (line 90)
44. - **Issue:** `usdcBalance: '0', // Placeholder` вҖ” USDC balance is hardcoded to `'0'`. Token approval scanning is also commented out as a future TODO. The threat detection only checks ETH balance vs tx count; no real heuristic for sweeper bots, approvals, EIP-7702.
45. - **Fix:** Integrate `ethers` token balance calls and/or Moralis/Alchemy API for token approvals.
46. 
47. ### рҹҹЎ Medium Priority
48. 
49. #### B7 вҖ” `@tiltcheck/suslink` is commented out in `discord-bot/index.ts` and `events.ts`
50. 
51. - **Files:** `apps/discord-bot/src/index.ts` (line 35), `events.ts` (line 17)
52. - **Issue:** `// import '@tiltcheck/suslink';` вҖ” the SusLink module is never initialized in the bot, so the auto-scan block in `events.ts` (lines 141-145) is dead code and the EventRouter never receives `link.scanned` events from SusLink.
53. - **Fix:** Uncomment the import and wire up the auto-scan config flag.
54. 
55. #### B8 вҖ” `events.ts` SusLink auto-scan block is hard-commented out
56. 
57. - **File:** `apps/discord-bot/src/handlers/events.ts` (lines 141вҖ“145)
58. - **Issue:** The entire `config.suslinkAutoScan` auto-scan block is inside a `/* ... */` comment block with only a stale comment inside. Link scanning in Discord messages is completely non-functional.
59. - **Fix:** Implement the block using the `LinkScanner` from `@tiltcheck/suslink`.
60. 
61. #### B9 вҖ” Trust alerts and trust adapter disabled in `index.ts`
62. 
63. - **File:** `apps/discord-bot/src/index.ts` (lines 79вҖ“81, 118вҖ“126)
64. - **Issue:** Both `TrustAlertsHandler.initialize()` and `startTrustAdapter()` are commented out with log messages saying "disabled". The trust event pipeline from EventRouter вҶ’ Discord is completely silent.
65. - **Fix:** Re-enable once the trust engine event signatures are stable.
66. 
67. #### B10 вҖ” `triviadrops/ai-questions.js` вҖ” AI question generation is a static bank with `isAIAvailable()` hardcoded to `false`
68. 
69. - **File:** `modules/triviadrops/ai-questions.js` (lines 18, 180вҖ“181)
70. - **Issue:** The `generateAIQuestion()` function ignores the AI path entirely. The `isAIAvailable()` function always returns `false`. Questions are pulled from a static bank of ~16 hardcoded questions with no difficulty/category diversity.
71. - **Fix:** Wire up OpenAI/Vercel AI SDK, or expand the static bank significantly.
72. 
73. #### B11 вҖ” `modules/stake/src/client.ts` вҖ” All three core methods are placeholder implementations
74. 
75. - **File:** `modules/stake/src/client.ts` (lines 50, 82, 116)
76. - **Issue:** `checkEligibility()`, `claimCode()`, and `getWagerRequirement()` all show `// Placeholder implementation`. Real API calls are commented out. Production use requires `STAKE_MOCK_API !== 'true'` which hits an unverified real endpoint.  
77. - **Fix:** Verify Stake API contract and implement real calls, or document this as a community-integration partner requirement.
78. 
79. #### B12 вҖ” `freespinscan` auto-approves "suspicious" promos without mod review
80. 
81. - **File:** `modules/freespinscan/src/index.ts` (line 148вҖ“151)
82. - **Issue:** `// Placeholder: auto-approve safe promos` вҖ” the code auto-fires `promo.approved` for any `suslinkScore === 'suspicious'` submission, bypassing the mod approval queue. "Suspicious" should go to review, not auto-approval.
83. - **Fix:** Only auto-approve `'safe'` scored promos; route `'suspicious'` to mod queue.
84. 
85. #### B13 вҖ” `qualifyfirst/engine.ts` event publisher is an optional stub never attached in production
86. 
87. - **File:** `modules/qualifyfirst/src/engine.ts` (lines 222вҖ“236)
88. - **Issue:** `publisher?.publish(...)` will silently do nothing if `attachPublisher()` is never called. No code in the bot or API ever calls `attachPublisher()`, so `survey.route.generated` and `survey.match.predicted` events are never emitted.
89. - **Fix:** Call `attachPublisher(eventRouter)` during initialization.
90. 
91. ### рҹҹў Low Priority / Code Quality
92. 
93. #### B14 вҖ” Multiple `as any` casts in bot service files masking type errors
94. 
95. - **Files:** `tilt-agent.ts` (Г—4), `tilt-events-handler.ts` (Г—4), `events.ts` (Г—1), `support.ts`, `lockvault.ts`, etc.
96. - **Issue:** Over a dozen `as any` casts used to suppress TypeScript errors. Some are benign (Elasticsearch SDK response shapes), others hide real type mismatches.
97. - **Fix:** Define proper interfaces for ES|QL responses and Discord channel types.
98. 
99. #### B15 вҖ” `database/tests/database.test.ts` вҖ” "placeholder methods" test
100.
```

</details>

211. ## рҹҡҖ STEPS TO DEPLOY
212. 
213. ### Prerequisites Checklist
214. 
215. ```bash
216. # Required env vars (minimum viable):
217. DISCORD_TOKEN=
218. DISCORD_CLIENT_ID=
219. DISCORD_GUILD_ID=
220. SUPABASE_URL=
221. SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY=
222. JWT_SECRET=
223. SOLANA_RPC_URL=
224. JUSTTHETIP_FEE_WALLET=
225. BACKEND_URL=https://api.tiltcheck.me  # or http://localhost:3001 for local
226. ```
227. 
228. ### Option A: Local Dev (recommended first step)
229. 
230. ```bash
231. # 1. Install deps
232. pnpm install
233. 
234. # 2. Copy env template and fill in required values
235. cp .env.template .env.local
236. 
237. # 3. Build all packages (order matters вҖ” dependencies first)
238. pnpm --filter @tiltcheck/types build
239. pnpm --filter @tiltcheck/event-router build
240. pnpm --filter @tiltcheck/db build
241. pnpm --filter @tiltcheck/auth build
242. 
243. # 4. Start API
244. pnpm --filter @tiltcheck/api dev   # вҶ’ http://localhost:3001
245. 
246. # 5. Start Discord bot (new terminal)
247. pnpm --filter @tiltcheck/discord-bot dev
248. 
249. # 6. Build Chrome Extension
250. cd apps/chrome-extension
251. node build.js
252. # Load dist/ folder as unpacked extension in chrome://extensions/
253. ```
254. 
255. ### Option B: VPS Deployment (Docker Compose)
256. 
257. ```bash
258. # On your VPS (85.209.95.175):
259. git clone <repo> /home/jme/tiltcheck-monorepo
260. cd /home/jme/tiltcheck-monorepo
261. 
262. # Set environment variables
263. cp .env .env.production
264. # Edit .env.production with production values
265. 
266. # Deploy all services
267. docker-compose up -d --build
268. 
269. # Services started:
270. # - discord-bot     вҶ’ port 8081 (health)
271. # - api             вҶ’ port 3001
272. # Configure Virtualmin reverse proxy:
273. #   tiltcheck.me/api вҶ’ localhost:3001
274. ```
275. 
276. ### Option C: Vercel (Frontend Only)
277. 
278. 1. Import GitHub repo in Vercel dashboard
279. 2. Set Root Directory вҶ’ `apps/web` (static site)
280. 3. Set Root Directory вҶ’ `apps/dashboard` (Next.js) вҖ” separate deployment
281. 4. Add env vars in Vercel project settings
282. 
283. ### Post-Deployment Verification
284. 
285. ```bash
286. # Bot health
287. curl http://localhost:8081/health
288. 
289. # API health
290. curl http://localhost:3001/health
291. 
292. # Register Discord slash commands
293. pnpm --filter @tiltcheck/discord-bot deploy-commands

### рҹҹЎ MEDIUM: SusLink Fetch Timeout вҖ” Invalid Option

**File:** `modules/suslink/src/scanner.ts` (line 247)

```typescript
fetch(url, { 
  ...options, 
  timeout: 5000,  // вҶҗ NOT A VALID FETCH API OPTION
  ... 
})
```

**Problem:** 
- `timeout` is not a valid fetch option in Node.js
- Silently ignored by browser/Node.js
- Uses `as any` to suppress TypeScript error
- Requests could hang indefinitely

**Fix:**
```typescript
const controller = new AbortController();
const timeout = setTimeout(() =\> controller.abort(), 5000);
const response = await fetch(url, { 
  ...options, 
  signal: controller.signal 
});
clearTimeout(timeout);
```

**Impact:** рҹҹЎ **MEDIUM**
- вҡ пёҸ Redirect following may hang
- вҡ пёҸ Resource exhaustion possible
- вҡ пёҸ No timeout protection

---

93.       await user.send(`${prefix} TiltCheck Intervention\n\n${message}`);
94.       console.log(`[TiltAgent] Intervention DM sent to ${userId} (${severity})`);
95.     } catch (err) {
96.       console.error(`[TiltAgent] Failed to DM user ${userId}:`, err);
97.     }
98.   });
99.   console.log('[TiltAgent] Scan loop active\n');
100.   if (process.env.ELASTIC_URL && process.env.ELASTIC_API_KEY) {
101.     const regsChannelId = process.env.REGULATIONS_ALERTS_CHANNEL_ID || '1447524353263665252';
102.     const regsGuildId = process.env.REGULATIONS_ALERTS_GUILD_ID || '1446973117472964620';
103. 
104.     startRegulationsNotifier(client, {
105.       elasticUrl: process.env.ELASTIC_URL,
106.       elasticApiKey: process.env.ELASTIC_API_KEY,
107.       channelId: regsChannelId,
108.       guildId: regsGuildId,
109.       intervalMs: Number(process.env.REGULATIONS_NOTIFIER_INTERVAL_MS || 6 * 60 * 60 * 1000),
110.       maxRowsInMessage: Number(process.env.REGULATIONS_NOTIFIER_MAX_ROWS || 15),
111.     });
112.   } else {
113.     console.log('[Regulations] Skipping notifier (Elastic not configured)');
114.   }
115. 
116.   initializeGameplayComplianceBridge(client);
117. 
118.   console.log('[LockVault] Starting background timer tasks...');
119.   startLockVaultBackgroundTasks();
120. 
121.   console.log('[DM] Registering direct message handler...');
122.   registerDMHandler(client);
123.   console.log('[DM] DM handler ready\n');
124. 
125.   console.log('[Adapter] Starting trust adapter...');
126.   startTrustAdapter({
127.     onFormatted: (formatted: string) => {
128.       console.log('[TrustAdapter]', formatted);
129.     },
130.   });
131.   console.log('[Adapter] Trust adapter ready\n');
132. 
133.   console.log('[Commands] Loading slash commands...');
134.   commandHandler.loadCommands();
135.   console.log('');
136. 
137.   console.log('[Events] Registering Discord events...');
138.   eventHandler.registerDiscordEvents();
139.   console.log('[Events] Discord events registered');
140. 
141.   console.log('[Events] Subscribing to EventRouter...');
142.   eventHandler.subscribeToEvents();
143.   console.log('[Events] EventRouter subscriptions active\n');
144. 
145.   console.log('[Discord] Connecting to Discord...');
146.   let ready = false;
147.   if (process.env.SKIP_DISCORD_LOGIN === 'true') {
148.     console.log('[Discord] CI mode - skipping Discord login');
149.     ready = true;
150.     try {
151.       fs.writeFileSync('/tmp/bot-ready', 'ready');
152.       console.log('[Health] Ready marker written');
153.     } catch (e) {
154.       console.error('[Health] Failed to write ready marker:', e);
155.     }
156.   } else {
157.     await client.login(config.discordToken);
158.     client.once('ready', () => {
159.       ready = true;
160.       console.log('[Discord] Connected and ready!');
161.       try {
162.         fs.writeFileSync('/tmp/bot-ready', 'ready');
163.         console.log('[Health] Ready marker written');
164.       } catch (e) {
165.         console.error('[Health] Failed to write ready marker:', e);
166.       }
167.     });
168.   }
169.   console.log('');
170. 
171.   const HEALTH_PORT = process.env.DISCORD_BOT_HEALTH_PORT || '8081';
172.   const PORT = parseInt(HEALTH_PORT, 10);
173. 
174.   const healthServer = http.createServer((req, res) => {
175.     if (req.url === '/health') {
176.       const body = JSON.stringify({
177.         service: 'discord-bot',
178.         ready,
179.         uptime: Math.round((Date.now() - startTime) / 1000),
180.         commands: commandHandler.getAllCommands().length
181.       });
182.       res.writeHead(200, { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' });
183.       res.end(body);
184.       return;
185.     }
186.     res.writeHead(404);
187.     res.end();
188.   });
189. 
190.   healthServer.listen(PORT, () => {
191.     console.log(`[Health] Bot health check listening on port ${PORT}`);
192.     console.log('[Bot] Ready');
193.   });
194. 
195.   healthServer.on('error', (err: NodeJS.ErrnoException) => {
196.     if (err.code === 'EADDRINUSE') {
197.       console.error(`Port ${PORT} is already in use.`);
198.       process.exit(1);
199.     }
200.     throw err;
201.   });
202. 
203.   // Tipping & Solana Consolidation
204.   let autoRefund: AutoRefundScheduler | undefined;
205.   let dMonitor: DepositMonitor | undefined;
206.   let tdMonitor: TokenDepositMonitor | undefined;
207. 
208.   if (config.botWalletPrivateKey) {
209.     console.log('[Tipping] Initializing consolidated credit system...');
210.     const solConnection = new Connection(config.solanaRpcUrl, 'confirmed');
211.     const botWallet = new BotWalletService(config.botWalletPrivateKey, solConnection);
212. 
213.     const dbClient = new DatabaseClient({
214.       url: config.supabaseUrl,
215.       apiKey: config.supabaseServiceRoleKey,
216.     });
217. 
218.     const cm = new CreditManager(dbClient);
219.     dMonitor = new DepositMonitor(solConnection, botWallet.address, cm);
220. 
221.     const swapService = new TokenSwapService(config.botWalletPrivateKey, solConnection);
222.     tdMonitor = new TokenDepositMonitor(solConnection, botWallet.address, cm, swapService);
223. 
224.     autoRefund = new AutoRefundScheduler(cm, botWallet.sendSOL.bind(botWallet), 12 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
225. 
226.     setCreditDeps(cm, dMonitor, botWallet, tdMonitor);
227. 
228.     dMonitor.start();
229.     tdMonitor.start();
230.     autoRefund.start();
231.     console.log('[Tipping] Credit system active\n');
232.   }
233. 
234.   const shutdown = async () => {
235.     console.log('\n[Bot] Shutting down gracefully...');
236. 
237.     stopTiltAgentLoop();
238.     stopRegulationsNotifier();
239.     stopLockVaultBackgroundTasks();
240. 
241.     if (autoRefund) autoRefund.stop();
242.     if (dMonitor) dMonitor.stop();
243.     if (tdMonitor) tdMonitor.stop();
244. 
245.     if (healthServer.listening) {
246.       healthServer.close();
247.     }
248. 
249.     if (client.isReady()) {
250.       console.log('[Bot] Destroying Discord client...');
251.       await client.destroy();
252.     }
253. 
254.     console.log('[Bot] Shutdown complete.');
255.     process.exit(0);
256.   };
257. 
258.   process.on('SIGINT', shutdown);
259.   process.on('SIGTERM', shutdown);
260. }
261. 
262. process.on('unhandledRejection', (error) => {
263.   console.error('[Bot] Unhandled rejection:', error);
264. });
265. 
266. main().catch((error) => {
267.   console.error('[Bot] Fatal error:', error);
268.   process.exit(1);
269. });
270. 
271. 
272. 
273.
```

```
1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. /**
3.  * Scan Command
4.  * 
5.  * Scans a URL for suspicious patterns using SusLink module.
6.  */
7. 
8. import { SlashCommandBuilder, ChatInputCommandInteraction } from 'discord.js';
9. import { suslink } from '@tiltcheck/suslink';
10. import { linkScanEmbed, errorEmbed, isValidUrl } from '@tiltcheck/discord-utils';
11. import type { Command } from '../types.js';
12. 
13. export const scan: Command = {
14.   data: new SlashCommandBuilder()
15.     .setName('scan')
16.     .setDescription('Scan a URL for suspicious patterns')
17.     .addStringOption((option) =>
18.       option
19.         .setName('url')
20.         .setDescription('The URL to scan')
21.         .setRequired(true)
22.     ) as SlashCommandBuilder,
23. 
24.   async execute(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
25.     await interaction.deferReply();
26. 
27.     const url = interaction.options.getString('url', true);
28. 
29.     // Validate URL
30.     if (!isValidUrl(url)) {
31.       const embed = errorEmbed(
32.         'Invalid URL',
33.         'Please provide a valid URL starting with http:// or https://'
34.       );
35.       await interaction.editReply({ embeds: [embed] });
36.       return;
37.     }
38. 
39.     try {
40.       // Scan the URL using SusLink
41.       const result = await suslink.scanUrl(url, interaction.user.id);
42. 
43.       // Create embed with results
44.       const embed = linkScanEmbed({
45.         url: result.url,
46.         riskLevel: result.riskLevel,
47.         reason: result.reason,
48.         scannedAt: result.scannedAt,
49.       });
50. 
51.       await interaction.editReply({ embeds: [embed] });
52.     } catch (error) {
53.       console.error('[ScanCommand] Error:', error);
54.       
55.       const embed = errorEmbed(
56.         'Scan Failed',
57.         'An error occurred while scanning the URL. Please try again.'
58.       );
59.       await interaction.editReply({ embeds: [embed] });
60.     }
61.   },
62. };
63.
```

</details>

74.   else color = 0xf04747; // Red (bad)

80.     .addFields(

203.   async execute(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
204.     const group = interaction.options.getSubcommandGroup(false);
205.     const subcommand = interaction.options.getSubcommand();
206. 
207.     if (subcommand === 'help') {
208.       await help.execute(interaction);
209.       return;
210.     }
211. 
212.     if (subcommand === 'ping') {
213.       await ping.execute(interaction);
214.       return;
215.     }
216. 
217.     if (subcommand === 'casino') {
218.       await casino.execute(interaction);
219.       return;
220.     }
221. 
222.     if (subcommand === 'setstate') {
223.       await setstate.execute(interaction);
224.       return;
225.     }
226. 
227.     if (subcommand === 'report') {
228.       if (!interaction.memberPermissions?.has(PermissionFlagsBits.ModerateMembers)) {
229.         await interaction.reply({ content: 'Mods only. This is not a toy.', ephemeral: true });
230.         return;
231.       }
232.       await report.execute(interaction);
233.       return;
234.     }
235. 
236.     if (group === 'link') {
237.       await linkCmd.execute(interaction);
238.       return;
239.     }
240. 
241.     if (group === 'buddy') {
242.       await buddy.execute(interaction);
243.       return;
244.     }
245. 
246.     if (subcommand === 'status') {
247.       await handleTiltStatus(interaction);
248.     } else if (subcommand === 'history') {
249.       await handleTiltHistory(interaction);
250.     } else if (subcommand === 'cooldown') {
251.       await handleCooldown(interaction);
252.     } else if (subcommand === 'diagnostics') {
253.       await handleDiagnostics(interaction);
254.     } else {
255.       await interaction.reply({ content: 'Unknown subcommand.', ephemeral: true });
256.     }
257.   },
258. };
259. 
260. async function handleTiltStatus(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
261.   const status = getUserTiltStatus(interaction.user.id);
262.   const cooldownStatus = getCooldownStatus(interaction.user.id);
263. 
264.   const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
265.     .setColor(status.onCooldown ? 0xFF6B6B : 0x00CED1)
266.     .setTitle('рҹ“Ҡ Tilt Status');
267. 
268.   if (status.onCooldown && cooldownStatus && cooldownStatus.endsAt) {
269.     const remaining = Math.ceil((cooldownStatus.endsAt - Date.now()) / 60000);
270.     const reason = cooldownStatus.reason || 'Unknown';
271.     embed.setDescription('вҸёпёҸ On cooldown')
272.       .addFields(
273.         { name: 'Time Remaining', value: `${remaining} minutes`, inline: true },
274.         { name: 'Reason', value: reason, inline: true },
275.         { name: 'Violations', value: `${cooldownStatus.violationCount}`, inline: true },
276.       );
277.   } else {
278.     embed.setDescription('вң… No active cooldown')
279.       .addFields(
280.         { name: 'Recent Signals', value: `${status.recentSignals.length} (last hour)`, inline: true },
281.         { name: 'Status', value: status.recentSignals.length >= 3 ? 'вҡ пёҸ Elevated' : 'вң… Normal', inline: true },
282.       );
283.   }
284. 
285.   // Show violation history if any
286.   const violationCount = getViolationHistory(interaction.user.id);
287.   if (violationCount > 0) {
288.     embed.addFields({ 
289.       name: 'Recent Violations (24h)', 
290.       value: `${violationCount} violations`, 
291.       inline: true
292.     });
293.   }
294. 
295.   embed.setFooter({ text: 'Use /tiltcheck cooldown to take a voluntary break' });
296. 
297.   await interaction.reply({ embeds: [embed], ephemeral: true });
298. }
299. 
300. async function handleTiltHistory(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
301.   const activity = getUserActivity(interaction.user.id);
302. 
303.   if (!activity) {
304.     await interaction.reply({ 
305.       content: 'рҹ“Ҡ No tilt history found. Keep it clean!',
306.       ephemeral: true 
307.     });
308.     return;
309.   }
310. 
311.   const recentMessages = activity.messages.slice(-10);
312. 
313.   const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
314.     .setColor(0x0099FF)
315.     .setTitle('рҹ“Ҳ Tilt History')
316.     .setDescription(`Activity tracking for ${interaction.user.username}`);
317. 
318.   if (recentMessages.length > 0) {
319.     const messageCount = recentMessages.length;
320.     const avgInterval = recentMessages.length > 1 
321.       ? (recentMessages[recentMessages.length - 1].timestamp - recentMessages[0].timestamp) / (messageCount - 1)
322.       : 0;
323.     
324.     embed.addFields({
325.       name: 'Recent Messages',
326.       value: `${messageCount} messages (avg ${Math.round(avgInterval / 1000)}s apart)`,
327.       inline: true,
328.     });
329.   }
330. 
331.   // Show loss streak if any
332.   if (activity.lossStreak > 0) {
333.     embed.addFields({
334.       name: 'Loss Streak',
335.       value: `${activity.lossStreak} consecutive losses`,
336.       inline: true,
337.     });
338.   }
339. 
340.   const violationCount = getViolationHistory(interaction.user.id);
341.   
342.   if (violationCount > 0) {
343.     embed.addFields({
344.       name: 'Cooldown Violations (24h)',
345.       value: `${violationCount} violations`,
346.       inline: true,
347.     });
348.   }
349. 
350.   embed.setFooter({ text: 'TiltCheck keeps you safe from yourself' });
351. 
352.   await interaction.reply({ embeds: [embed], ephemeral: true });
353. }
354. 
355. async function handleCooldown(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
356.   const duration = interaction.options.getInteger('duration') || 15;
357. 
358.   if (duration < 5 || duration > 1440) {
359.     await interaction.reply({ 
360.       content: 'вқҢ Duration must be between 5 and 1440 minutes (24 hours)',
361.       ephemeral: true 
362.     });
363.     return;
364.   }
365. 
366.   const existing = isOnCooldown(interaction.user.id);
367. 
368.   if (existing) {
369.     const status = getCooldownStatus(interaction.user.id);
370.     const remaining = status && status.endsAt ? Math.ceil((status.endsAt - Date.now()) / 60000) : 0;
371.     
372.     await interaction.reply({ 
373.       content: `вҸёпёҸ You're already on cooldown for ${remaining} more minutes`,
374.       ephemeral: true 
375.     });
376.     return;
377.   }
378. 
379.   startCooldown(
380.     interaction.user.id,
381.     `Voluntary cooldown by ${interaction.user.username}`,
382.     duration * 60 * 1000 // Convert minutes to milliseconds
383.   );
384. 
385.   const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
386.     .setColor(0x00CED1)
387.     .setTitle('вҸёпёҸ Cooldown Started')
388.     .setDescription(`Taking a ${duration}-minute break. Smart move.`)
389.     .addFields(
390.       { name: 'Duration', value: `${duration} minutes`, inline: true },
391.       { name: 'Expires', value: `<t:${Math.floor((Date.now() + duration * 60000) / 1000)}:R>`, inline: true },
392.     )
393.     .setFooter({ text: 'Violations will extend your cooldown automatically' });
394. 
395.   await interaction.reply({ embeds: [embed] });
396. }
397. 
398. async function handleDiagnostics(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
399.   // Simple admin check (can be expanded)
400.   const isAdmin = interaction.memberPermissions?.has('Administrator') || interaction.user.id === interaction.guild?.ownerId;
401.   
402.   if (!isAdmin) {
403.     await interaction.reply({ content: 'вқҢ Only administrators can view system diagnostics.', ephemeral: true });
404.     return;
405.   }
406. 
407.   const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
408.     .setColor(0x9B59B6)
409.     .setTitle('вҡҷпёҸ TiltCheck Diagnostics')
410.     .addFields(
411.       { name: 'Service Status', value: 'вң… Operational', inline: true },
412.       { name: 'Detection Engine', value: 'вң… Active', inline: true },
413.       { name: 'Event Router', value: 'вң… Connected', inline: true },
414.       { name: 'Uptime', value: `${Math.floor(process.uptime() / 60)} minutes`, inline: true },
415.       { name: 'Memory Usage', value: `${Math.round(process.memoryUsage().heapUsed / 1024 / 1024)}MB`, inline: true },
416.     );
417. 
418.   await interaction.reply({ embeds: [embed], ephemeral: true });
419. }
420.
```

1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. import { SlashCommandBuilder, ChatInputCommandInteraction, EmbedBuilder } from 'discord.js';
3. import { db } from '@tiltcheck/database';
4. import type { Command } from '../types.js';
5. 
6. export const casino: Command = {
7.   data: new SlashCommandBuilder()
8.     .setName('casino')
9.     .setDescription('Get trust and fairness data for a casino')
10.     .addStringOption(option =>
11.       option
12.         .setName('domain')
13.         .setDescription('Casino domain (e.g., stake.com)')
14.         .setRequired(true)
15.     ),
16. 
17.   async execute(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
18.     await interaction.deferReply();
19.     const domain = interaction.options.getString('domain', true).toLowerCase();
20. 
21.     try {
22.       const data = await db.getCasino(domain);
23. 
24.       if (!data) {
25.         await interaction.editReply({
26.           content: `вқҢ No data found for **${domain}**.\n\nTry domains like \`stake.com\`, \`rollbit.com\`, or \`duelbits.com\`.`
27.         });
28.         return;
29.       }
30. 
31.       const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
32.         .setTitle(`рҹҺ° ${data.name} (${data.domain})`)
33.         .setColor(data.status === 'active' ? 0x00FF00 : 0xFF0000)
34.         .setDescription(`Trust and fairness data for ${data.name}.`)
35.         .addFields(
36.           { name: 'Status', value: data.status.toUpperCase(), inline: true },
37.           { name: 'Claimed RTP', value: data.claimed_rtp ? `${data.claimed_rtp}%` : 'N/A', inline: true },
38.           { name: 'Verified RTP', value: data.verified_rtp ? `${data.verified_rtp}%` : 'N/A', inline: true },
39.         );
40. 
41.       if (data.license_info) {
42.         const license = typeof data.license_info === 'string' 
43.           ? JSON.parse(data.license_info) 
44.           : data.license_info;
45.         
46.         const licenseDetails = Object.entries(license)
47.           .map(([k, v]) => `вҖў **${k}:** ${v}`)
48.           .join('\n');
49.           
50.         embed.addFields({ name: 'рҹ“ң License Info', value: licenseDetails || 'No details', inline: false });
51.       }
52. 
53.       embed.setFooter({ text: 'TiltCheck Trust Engine вҖў Verified Data' });
54.       embed.setTimestamp(new Date(data.updated_at));
55.

57.     } catch (error) {
58.       console.error('[Casino] Error:', error);
59.       await interaction.editReply({ content: 'вқҢ Failed to fetch casino data.' });
60.     }

17.         .setRequired(true)

24.           { name: 'Flag Rain Farmer', value: 'flag_farmer' }
25.         ))

27.       option.setName('reason')
28.         .setDescription('Reason for the action')
29.         .setRequired(true))
30.     .addStringOption(option =>
31.       option.setName('evidence')
32.         .setDescription('Link to screenshot or message (optional)')
33.         .setRequired(false)),

35.   async execute(interaction: any) {
36.     const target = interaction.options.getUser('target');
37.     const action = interaction.options.getString('action');
38.     const reason = interaction.options.getString('reason');
39.     const evidence = interaction.options.getString('evidence');
40.     const moderator = interaction.user;
41. 
42.     // Defer reply since DB operations might take a moment
43.     await interaction.deferReply({ ephemeral: true });
44. 
45.     try {
46.       const backendUrl = process.env.BACKEND_URL;
47.       const internalApiSecret = process.env.INTERNAL_API_SECRET;
48. 
49.       if (!backendUrl) {
50.         throw new Error('BACKEND_URL is not configured');
51.       }
52.       if (!internalApiSecret) {
53.         throw new Error('INTERNAL_API_SECRET is not configured');
54.       }
55. 
56.       // Send to your backend API which handles the DB insertion
57.       const response = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/api/mod/report`, {
58.         method: 'POST',
59.         headers: {
60.           'Content-Type': 'application/json',
61.           'Authorization': `Bearer ${internalApiSecret}`,
62.         },
63.         body: JSON.stringify({
64.           targetId: target.id,
65.           targetUsername: target.username,
66.           moderatorId: moderator.id,
67.           actionType: action,
68.           reason,
69.           evidenceUrl: evidence
70.         })
71.       });
72. 
73.       if (!response.ok) {
74.         throw new Error(`API Error: ${response.statusText}`);
75.       }
76. 
77.       const result = await response.json();
78. 
79.       await interaction.editReply({
80.         content: `вң… **Report Logged Successfully**\n\n**Target:** ${target.tag}\n**Action:** ${action.toUpperCase().replace('_', ' ')}\n**Case ID:** \`${result.id || 'Pending'}\``
81.       });
82. 
83.     } catch (error) {
84.       console.error('Report command error:', error);
85.       await interaction.editReply({
86.         content: `вқҢ Failed to log report. Please check the backend connection.`
87.       });
88.     }
89.   }
90. };

1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. /**
3.  * Link Safety Command
4.  * Combines link scanning and promo management
5.  */
6. 
7. import { SlashCommandBuilder, ChatInputCommandInteraction } from 'discord.js';
8. import { suslink } from '@tiltcheck/suslink';
9. import { linkScanEmbed, errorEmbed, isValidUrl } from '@tiltcheck/discord-utils';
10. import type { Command } from '../types.js';
11. 
12. export const linkCmd: Command = {
13.   data: new SlashCommandBuilder()
14.     .setName('link')
15.     .setDescription('Link scanning for suspicious patterns')
16.     .addSubcommand(sub =>
17.       sub
18.         .setName('scan')
19.         .setDescription('Scan a URL for suspicious patterns')
20.         .addStringOption(opt =>
21.           opt.setName('url').setDescription('The URL to scan').setRequired(true)
22.         )
23.     ),
24. 
25.   async execute(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
26.     const subcommand = interaction.options.getSubcommand();
27. 
28.     switch (subcommand) {
29.       case 'scan':
30.         await handleScan(interaction);
31.         break;
32.       default:
33.         await interaction.reply({ content: 'Unknown command', ephemeral: true });
34.     }
35.   },
36. };
37. 
38. async function handleScan(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
39.   await interaction.deferReply();
40. 
41.   const url = interaction.options.getString('url', true);
42. 
43.   if (!isValidUrl(url)) {
44.     const embed = errorEmbed(
45.       'Invalid URL',
46.       'Please provide a valid URL starting with http:// or https://'
47.     );
48.     await interaction.editReply({ embeds: [embed] });
49.     return;
50.   }
51. 
52.   try {
53.     const result = await suslink.scanUrl(url, interaction.user.id);
54. 
55.     const embed = linkScanEmbed({
56.       url: result.url,
57.       riskLevel: result.riskLevel,
58.       reason: result.reason,
59.       scannedAt: result.scannedAt,
60.     });
61. 
62.     await interaction.editReply({ embeds: [embed] });
63.   } catch (error) {
64.     console.error('[SusLink] Scan error:', error);
65.     const embed = errorEmbed(
66.       'Scan Failed',
67.       'An error occurred while scanning the URL. Please try again.'
68.     );
69.     await interaction.editReply({ embeds: [embed] });
70.   }
71. }
```

1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. 
3. import { SlashCommandBuilder, ChatInputCommandInteraction, EmbedBuilder } from 'discord.js';
4. import type { Command } from '../types.js';
5. import { db } from '@tiltcheck/database';
6. import { PublicKey } from '@solana/web3.js';
7. 
8. export const linkwallet: Command = {
9.   data: new SlashCommandBuilder()
10.     .setName('linkwallet')
11.     .setDescription('Link your Solana wallet address for payouts and juice drops')
12.     .addStringOption(opt =>
13.       opt
14.         .setName('address')
15.         .setDescription('Your Solana wallet address (e.g., Phantom, Trust, Solflare)')
16.         .setRequired(true)
17.     ),
18.   async execute(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
19.     const address = interaction.options.getString('address', true);
20. 
21.     // Validate Solana Address
22.     try {
23.       new PublicKey(address);
24.     } catch {
25.       await interaction.reply({ content: 'вқҢ Invalid Solana address. Please check and try again.', ephemeral: true });
26.       return;
27.     }
28. 
29.     await interaction.deferReply({ ephemeral: true });
30. 
31.     try {
32.       if (db.isConnected()) {
33.         await db.upsertDegenIdentity({
34.           discord_id: interaction.user.id,
35.           primary_external_address: address,
36.           username: interaction.user.username // Sync username while we are at it
37.         });
38. 
39.         const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
40.           .setColor(0x22d3a6)
41.           .setTitle('рҹ”— Wallet Linked')
42.           .setDescription(`Successfully linked your wallet to the TiltCheck Hub.
43. 
44. **Address:** `${address}`
45. 
46. You are now ready to catch some juice! рҹ§ғ`)
47.           .setFooter({ text: 'Manage more settings at dashboard.tiltcheck.me' });
48. 
49.         await interaction.editReply({ embeds: [embed] });
50.       } else {
51.         throw new Error('Database connection failed');
52.       }
53.     } catch (error) {
54.       console.error('[LinkWallet] Error:', error);
55.       await interaction.editReply({ content: 'вқҢ Failed to save wallet address. Please try again later.' });
56.     }
57.   },
58. };

1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. import { SlashCommandBuilder, ChatInputCommandInteraction } from 'discord.js';
3. import { getAlertService } from '../services/alert-service.js';
4. import type { Command } from '../types.js';
5. 
6. const SUPPORT_CHANNEL_ID = '1437295074856927363';
7. const OWNER_MENTION = '<@jmenichole>';
8. 
9. export const support: Command = {
10.   data: new SlashCommandBuilder()
11.     .setName('support')
12.     .setDescription('Request help from TiltCheck support')
13.     .addStringOption(option =>
14.       option.setName('topic').setDescription('What do you need help with?').setRequired(false)
15.     )
16.     .addStringOption(option =>
17.       option.setName('message').setDescription('Describe your issue (optional)').setRequired(false)
18.     ),
19. 
20.   async execute(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
21.     const topic = interaction.options.getString('topic') || 'General Support';
22.     const message = interaction.options.getString('message') || '';
23. 
24.     // Send a message in the support channel pinging the owner
25.     const guild = interaction.guild;
26.     if (!guild) {
27.       await interaction.reply({ content: 'вқҢ This command can only be used in a server.', ephemeral: true });
28.       return;
29.     }
30.     const channel = guild.channels.cache.get(SUPPORT_CHANNEL_ID);
31.     if (!channel || !('send' in channel)) {
32.       await interaction.reply({ content: 'вқҢ Support channel not found.', ephemeral: true });
33.       return;
34.     }
35. 
36.     // Post to support channel via traditional message
37.     const supportMsg = `рҹ”” **Support Request** from <@${interaction.user.id}> ${OWNER_MENTION}\nрҹ“Ң **Topic:** ${topic}${message ? `\nрҹ’¬ **Message:** ${message}` : ''}`;
38.     await (channel as any).send({ content: supportMsg });
39. 
40.     // Also post to support alerts channel via AlertService
41.     const alertService = getAlertService();
42.     if (alertService) {
43.       try {
44.         await alertService.postSupportTicket({
45.           userId: interaction.user.id,
46.           username: interaction.user.username,
47.           topic,
48.           message: message || '(No additional details provided)',
49.           status: 'open',
50.         });
51.       } catch (error) {
52.         console.error('[Support] Error posting support ticket alert:', error);
53.       }
54.     }
55. 
56.     await interaction.reply({ content: 'вң… Support request sent! Someone will be with you soon.', ephemeral: true });
57.   },
58. };
59.
```

1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. /**
3.  * Cooldown & Tilt Management Commands
4.  * Safety features for preventing tilt-driven losses
5.  */
6. 
7. import { SlashCommandBuilder, ChatInputCommandInteraction, EmbedBuilder } from 'discord.js';
8. import type { Command } from '../types.js';
9. import { 
10.   startCooldown, 
11.   isOnCooldown, 
12.   getCooldownStatus, 
13.   getViolationHistory,
14.   getUserTiltStatus,
15.   getUserActivity,
16. } from '@tiltcheck/tiltcheck-core';
17. 
18. export const cooldown: Command = {
19.   data: new SlashCommandBuilder()
20.     .setName('cooldown')
21.     .setDescription('Start a voluntary cooldown period')
22.     .addIntegerOption(opt =>
23.       opt
24.         .setName('duration')
25.         .setDescription('Duration in minutes (default: 15)')
26.         .setRequired(false)
27.     ),
28. 
29.   async execute(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
30.     const duration = interaction.options.getInteger('duration') || 15;
31. 
32.     if (duration < 5 || duration > 1440) {
33.       await interaction.reply({ 
34.         content: 'вқҢ Duration must be between 5 and 1440 minutes (24 hours)',
35.         ephemeral: true 
36.       });
37.       return;
38.     }
39. 
40.     const existing = isOnCooldown(interaction.user.id);
41. 
42.     if (existing) {
43.       const status = getCooldownStatus(interaction.user.id);
44.       const remaining = status && status.endsAt ? Math.ceil((status.endsAt - Date.now()) / 60000) : 0;
45.       
46.       await interaction.reply({ 
47.         content: `вҸёпёҸ You're already on cooldown for ${remaining} more minutes`,
48.         ephemeral: true 
49.       });
50.       return;
51.     }
52. 
53.     startCooldown(
54.       interaction.user.id,
55.       `Voluntary cooldown by ${interaction.user.username}`,
56.       duration * 60 * 1000 // Convert minutes to milliseconds
57.     );
58. 
59.     const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
60.       .setColor(0x00CED1)
61.       .setTitle('вҸёпёҸ Cooldown Started')
62.       .setDescription(`Taking a ${duration}-minute break. Smart move.`)
63.       .addFields(
64.         { name: 'Duration', value: `${duration} minutes`, inline: true },
65.         { name: 'Expires', value: `<t:${Math.floor((Date.now() + duration * 60000) / 1000)}:R>`, inline: true },
66.       )
67.       .setFooter({ text: 'Violations will extend your cooldown automatically' });
68. 
69.     await interaction.reply({ embeds: [embed] });
70.   },
71. };
72. 
73. export const tilt: Command = {
74.   data: new SlashCommandBuilder()
75.     .setName('tilt')
76.     .setDescription('Check your tilt status and history')
77.     .addSubcommand(sub =>
78.       sub
79.         .setName('status')
80.         .setDescription('Check your current tilt status')
81.     )
82.     .addSubcommand(sub =>
83.       sub
84.         .setName('history')
85.         .setDescription('View your tilt detection history')
86.     ),
87. 
88.   async execute(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
89.     const subcommand = interaction.options.getSubcommand();
90. 
91.     if (subcommand === 'status') {
92.       await handleTiltStatus(interaction);
93.     } else if (subcommand === 'history') {
94.       await handleTiltHistory(interaction);
95.     }
96.   },
97. };
98. 
99. async function handleTiltStatus(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
100.   const status = getUserTiltStatus(interaction.user.id);
101.   const cooldownStatus = getCooldownStatus(interaction.user.id);
102. 
103.   const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
104.     .setColor(status.onCooldown ? 0xFF6B6B : 0x00CED1)
105.     .setTitle('рҹ“Ҡ Tilt Status');
106. 
107.   if (status.onCooldown && cooldownStatus && cooldownStatus.endsAt) {
108.     const remaining = Math.ceil((cooldownStatus.endsAt - Date.now()) / 60000);
109.     const reason = cooldownStatus.reason || 'Unknown';
110.     embed.setDescription('вҸёпёҸ On cooldown')
111.       .addFields(
112.         { name: 'Time Remaining', value: `${remaining} minutes`, inline: true },
113.         { name: 'Reason', value: reason, inline: true },
114.         { name: 'Violations', value: `${cooldownStatus.violationCount}`, inline: true },
115.       );
116.   } else {
117.     embed.setDescription('вң… No active cooldown')
118.       .addFields(

139. async function handleTiltHistory(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {

148.   }

151. 
152.   const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
153.     .setColor(0x0099FF)
154.     .setTitle('рҹ“Ҳ Tilt History')
155.     .setDescription(`Activity tracking for ${interaction.user.username}`);
156. 
157.   if (recentMessages.length > 0) {
158.     const messageCount = recentMessages.length;
159.     const avgInterval = recentMessages.length > 1 
160.       ? (recentMessages[recentMessages.length - 1].timestamp - recentMessages[0].timestamp) / (messageCount - 1)
161.       : 0;
162.     
163.     embed.addFields({
164.       name: 'Recent Messages',
165.       value: `${messageCount} messages (avg ${Math.round(avgInterval / 1000)}s apart)`,
166.       inline: true,
167.     });
168.   }
169. 
170.   // Show loss streak if any
171.   if (activity.lossStreak > 0) {
172.     embed.addFields({
173.       name: 'Loss Streak',
174.       value: `${activity.lossStreak} consecutive losses`,
175.       inline: true,
176.     });
177.   }
178. 
179.   const violationCount = getViolationHistory(interaction.user.id);
180.   
181.   if (violationCount > 0) {
182.     embed.addFields({
183.       name: 'Cooldown Violations (24h)',
184.       value: `${violationCount} violations`,
185.       inline: true,
186.     });
187.   }
188.

190.

2. /**
3.  * Terms Command
4.  * Displays TiltCheck Terms of Service & Privacy links and tracks acceptance.
5.  */
6. import { SlashCommandBuilder, ChatInputCommandInteraction, EmbedBuilder, ActionRowBuilder, ButtonBuilder, ButtonStyle } from 'discord.js';
7. import type { Command } from '../types.js';
8. import { db } from '@tiltcheck/database';

10. import path from 'path';
11. 
12. const TERMS_STORE = path.join(process.cwd(), 'data', 'terms-acceptance.json');
13. const VERSION = '1.0';
14. 
15. interface TermsAcceptance { userId: string; username: string; acceptedAt: string; version: string; }
16. function ensureStoreDir() { const dir = path.dirname(TERMS_STORE); if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true }); }
17. function loadAcceptances(): TermsAcceptance[] { ensureStoreDir(); if (!fs.existsSync(TERMS_STORE)) return []; try { return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(TERMS_STORE, 'utf8')); } catch { return []; } }
18. function saveAcceptance(a: TermsAcceptance) { const all = loadAcceptances().filter(x => x.userId !== a.userId); all.push(a); fs.writeFileSync(TERMS_STORE, JSON.stringify(all, null, 2)); }
19. export function hasAcceptedTerms(uid: string): boolean { return loadAcceptances().some(a => a.userId === uid); }
20.

37.           { name: 'Acceptance', value: 'Use `/terms accept` after reading.' },

43.       return;
44.     }
45.     if (sub === 'accept') {

61.         if (btn.customId === 'terms_accept_confirm') {

17. } from '@tiltcheck/justthetip';

19. import { isOnCooldown } from '@tiltcheck/tiltcheck-core';
20. import { db } from '@tiltcheck/database';
21. import { Connection } from '@solana/web3.js';
22. 
23. const SOLANA_RPC_URL = process.env.SOLANA_RPC_URL || 'https://api.mainnet-beta.solana.com';
24. const connection = new Connection(SOLANA_RPC_URL, 'confirmed');
25. 
26. export const justthetip: Command = {
27.   data: new SlashCommandBuilder()
28.     .setName('justthetip')
29.     .setDescription('Non-custodial Solana tipping')
30.     .addSubcommand(sub =>
31.       sub
32.         .setName('wallet')
33.         .setDescription('Manage your wallet')
34.         .addStringOption(opt =>
35.           opt
36.             .setName('action')
37.             .setDescription('Wallet action')
38.             .setRequired(true)
39.             .addChoices(
40.               { name: 'View', value: 'view' },
41.               { name: 'Register (Magic Link)', value: 'register-magic' },
42.               { name: 'Register (External)', value: 'register-external' },
43.             )
44.         )
45.         .addStringOption(opt =>
46.           opt
47.             .setName('address')
48.             .setDescription('Wallet address (for external registration)')
49.             .setRequired(false)
50.         )
51.     )
52.     .addSubcommand(sub =>
53.       sub
54.         .setName('tip')
55.         .setDescription('Send a tip to another user')
56.         .addUserOption(opt =>
57.           opt
58.             .setName('user')
59.             .setDescription('User to tip')
60.             .setRequired(true)
61.         )
62.         .addStringOption(opt =>
63.           opt
64.             .setName('amount')
65.             .setDescription('Amount (e.g., "5 sol", "$10", "all")')
66.             .setRequired(true)
67.         )
68.     )
69.     .addSubcommand(sub =>
70.       sub
71.         .setName('balance')
72.         .setDescription('Check your wallet balance')
73.     )
74.     .addSubcommand(sub =>
75.       sub
76.         .setName('pending')
77.         .setDescription('View pending tips sent to you')
78.     ),
79. 
80.   async execute(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
81.     try {
82.       const subcommand = interaction.options.getSubcommand(false);
83. 
84.       if (!subcommand) {
85.         await interaction.reply({
86.           content: 'вқҢ Please specify a subcommand:\n' +
87.             'вҖў `/justthetip wallet` - Manage your wallet\n' +
88.             'вҖў `/justthetip tip` - Send a tip\n' +
89.             'вҖў `/justthetip balance` - Check balance\n' +
90.             'вҖў `/justthetip pending` - View pending tips',
91.           ephemeral: true
92.         });
93.         return;
94.       }
95. 
96.       switch (subcommand) {
97.         case 'wallet':
98.           await handleWallet(interaction);
99.           break;
100.         case 'tip':
101.           await handleTip(interaction);
102.           break;
103.         case 'balance':
104.           await handleBalance(interaction);
105.           break;
106.         case 'pending':
107.           await handlePending(interaction);
108.           break;
109.         default:
110.           await interaction.reply({ content: 'Unknown command', ephemeral: true });
111.       }
112.     } catch (error) {
113.       console.error('[JUSTTHETIP] Command error:', error);
114.       const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'An unexpected error occurred';
115.       
116.       if (interaction.deferred || interaction.replied) {
117.         await interaction.editReply({ content: `вқҢ Error: ${errorMessage}` });
118.       } else {
119.         await interaction.reply({ content: `вқҢ Error: ${errorMessage}`, ephemeral: true });
120.       }
121.     }
122.   },
123. };
124. 
125. async function handleWallet(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
126.   const action = interaction.options.getString('action', true);
127. 
128.   if (action === 'view') {
129.     const wallet = getWallet(interaction.user.id);
130.     
131.     if (!wallet) {
132.       await interaction.reply({
133.         content: 'вқҢ No wallet registered. Use `/justthetip wallet register-external`',
134.         ephemeral: true,
135.       });
136.       return;
137.     }
138. 
139.     const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
140.       .setColor(0x00FF00)
141.       .setTitle('рҹ’і Your Wallet')
142.       .addFields(
143.         { name: 'Address', value: `\`${wallet.address}\``, inline: false },
144.         { name: 'Type', value: wallet.type, inline: true },
145.         { name: 'Registered', value: `<t:${Math.floor(wallet.registeredAt / 1000)}:R>`, inline: true },
146.       );
147. 
148.     await interaction.reply({ embeds: [embed], ephemeral: true });
149.   } else if (action === 'register-magic') {
150.     if (db.isConnected()) {
151.       const identity = await db.getDegenIdentity(interaction.user.id);
152.       if (identity?.magic_address) {
153.         await interaction.reply({
154.           content: `вң… You already have a **Degen Identity** wallet linked:\n\`${identity.magic_address}\``,
155.           ephemeral: true,
156.         });
157.         return;
158.       }
159.     }
160. 
161.     const dashboardUrl = process.env.DASHBOARD_URL || 'https://tiltcheck.me/dashboard';
162.     const linkUrl = `${dashboardUrl}?action=link-magic&userId=${interaction.user.id}`;
163.     
164.     const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
165.       .setColor(0x8A2BE2)
166.       .setTitle('вңЁ Register with Magic Link')
167.       .setDescription('Connect your email to create a secure **Soft-Custody** wallet for tipping and vaulting.')
168.       .addFields(
169.         { name: 'Step 1', value: `[Click here to open Dashboard](${linkUrl})` },
170.         { name: 'Step 2', value: 'Login with your Email' },
171.         { name: 'Step 3', value: 'Link your Discord account' }
172.       )
173.       .setFooter({ text: 'TiltCheck вҖў Trust & Safety' });
174. 
175.     await interaction.reply({ embeds: [embed], ephemeral: true });
176.   } else if (action === 'register-external') {
177.     const address = interaction.options.getString('address');
178.     
179.     if (!address) {
180.       await interaction.reply({
181.         content: 'вқҢ Please provide your Solana wallet address:\n' +
182.           '`/justthetip wallet register-external address:<your-address>`\n\n' +
183.           'Find your address in Phantom, Solflare, or other Solana wallets.',
184.         ephemeral: true,
185.       });
186.       return;
187.     }
188. 
189.     try {
190.       const wallet = await registerExternalWallet(interaction.user.id, address);
191.       
192.       const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
193.         .setColor(0x00FF00)
194.         .setTitle('вң… Wallet Registered!')
195.         .setDescription('Your external wallet has been connected')
196.         .addFields(
197.           { name: 'Address', value: `\`${wallet.address}\``, inline: false },
198.           { name: 'Type', value: 'External', inline: true },
199.         )
200.         .setFooter({ text: 'You can now send and receive tips!' });
201. 
202.       await interaction.reply({ embeds: [embed], ephemeral: true });
203.     } catch (error) {
204.       await interaction.reply({
205.         content: `вқҢ ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Invalid wallet address'}`,
206.         ephemeral: true,
207.       });
208.     }
209.   }
210. }
211. 
212. async function handleTip(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
213.   await interaction.deferReply();
214. 
215.   // Check if sender is on cooldown
216.   if (isOnCooldown(interaction.user.id)) {
217.     await interaction.editReply({
218.       content: 'рҹҡ« You\'re on cooldown and cannot send tips right now. Take a break.',
219.     });
220.     return;
221.   }
222. 
223.   // Check sender has wallet
224.   if (!hasWallet(interaction.user.id)) {
225.     await interaction.editReply({
226.       content: 'вқҢ You need to register a wallet first!\n' +
227.         'Use `/justthetip wallet register-external` to connect your Solana wallet.',
228.     });
229.     return;
230.   }
231. 
232.   const recipient = interaction.options.getUser('user', true);
233.   const amountInput = interaction.options.getString('amount', true);
234. 
235.   // Don't allow self-tipping
236.   if (recipient.id === interaction.user.id) {
237.     await interaction.editReply({
238.       content: 'вқҢ You cannot tip yourself!',
239.     });
240.     return;
241.   }
242. 
243.   // Parse amount with NLP
244.   const parseResult = parseAmount(amountInput);
245.   
246.   if (!parseResult.success || !parseResult.data) {
247.     await interaction.editReply({
248.       content: `вқҢ ${parseResult.error}\n\n` +
249.         `${parseResult.suggestions?.join('\n') || ''}`,
250.     });
251.     return;
252.   }
253. 
254.   const parsedAmount = parseResult.data;
255. 
256.   // Handle confirmation if needed
257.   if (parseResult.needsConfirmation && parseResult.confirmationPrompt) {
258.     const confirmButton = new ButtonBuilder()
259.       .setCustomId(`tip_confirm_sol_${recipient.id}_${parsedAmount.value}`)
260.       .setLabel(`Yes, ${parsedAmount.value} SOL`)
261.       .setStyle(ButtonStyle.Success);
262. 
263.     const cancelButton = new ButtonBuilder()
264.       .setCustomId('tip_cancel')
265.       .setLabel('Cancel')
266.       .setStyle(ButtonStyle.Danger);
267. 
268.     const row = new ActionRowBuilder<ButtonBuilder>().addComponents(confirmButton, cancelButton);
269. 
270.     await interaction.editReply({
271.       content: `вҡ пёҸ **Confirmation Needed**\n\n${parseResult.confirmationPrompt}`,
272.       components: [row],
273.     });
274.     return;
275.   }
276. 
277.   // Check if recipient has wallet
278.   const recipientWallet = getWallet(recipient.id);
279.   const senderWallet = getWallet(interaction.user.id);
280.   
281.   if (!senderWallet) {
282.     throw new Error('Sender wallet not found');
283.   }
284. 
285.   if (!recipientWallet) {
286.     await interaction.editReply({
287.       content: `вҡ пёҸ ${recipient} doesn't have a wallet registered yet.\n` +
288.         'Your tip will be held for 24 hours. They can claim it by registering a wallet.',
289.     });
290.     
291.     // We can't really "hold" a non-custodial tip without the sender signing something,
292.     // so we just log it as a pending intent for now.
293.     return;
294.   }
295. 
296.   // Generate Solana Pay deep link
297.   try {
298.     const { url, reference } = await createTipWithFeeRequest(
299.       connection,
300.       senderWallet.address,
301.       recipientWallet.address,
302.       parsedAmount.value,
303.       `TiltCheck Tip to ${recipient.username}`
304.     );
305. 
306.     // Track the transaction by reference
307.     trackTransactionByReference(
308.       reference,
309.       interaction.user.id,
310.       'tip',
311.       parsedAmount.value,
312.       recipient.id
313.     );
314. 
315.     // Create button with Solana Pay deep link
316.     const payButton = new ButtonBuilder()
317.       .setLabel('рҹ’ё Open in Wallet')
318.       .setStyle(ButtonStyle.Link)
319.       .setURL(url);
320. 
321.     const row = new ActionRowBuilder<ButtonBuilder>().addComponents(payButton);
322. 
323.     const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
324.       .setColor(0x00FF00)
325.       .setTitle('рҹ’ё Tip Ready to Send')
326.       .setDescription(
327.         `**Recipient:** ${recipient}\n` +
328.         `**Amount:** ${formatAmount(parsedAmount)}\n` +
329.         `**Fee:** 0.0007 SOL (~$0.07)\n\n` +
330.         '**Tap the button below** to open in your wallet:\n' +
331.         'вҖў Phantom\n' +
332.         'вҖў Solflare\n' +
333.         'вҖў Backpack\n' +
334.         'вҖў Any Solana wallet\n\n' +
335.         'Your device will ask which wallet to use! рҹ“ұ'
336.       )
337.       .setFooter({ text: 'Powered by Solana Pay' });
338. 
339.     await interaction.editReply({ 
340.       embeds: [embed],
341.       components: [row],
342.     });
343. 
344.   } catch (error) {
345.     await interaction.editReply({
346.       content: `вқҢ Failed to create payment request: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error'}`,
347.     });
348.   }
349. }
350. 
351. async function handleBalance(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
352.   await interaction.deferReply({ ephemeral: true });
353. 
354.   if (!hasWallet(interaction.user.id)) {
355.     await interaction.editReply({
356.       content: 'вқҢ No wallet registered. Use `/justthetip wallet register-external`',
357.     });
358.     return;
359.   }
360. 
361.   try {
362.     const balance = await getWalletBalance(interaction.user.id);
363.     const wallet = getWallet(interaction.user.id);
364. 
365.     const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
366.       .setColor(0x0099FF)
367.       .setTitle('рҹ’° Wallet Balance')
368.       .addFields(
369.         { name: 'Balance', value: `${balance.toFixed(6)} SOL`, inline: true },
370.         { name: 'Address', value: `\`${wallet?.address}\``, inline: false },
371.       );
372. 
373.     await interaction.editReply({ embeds: [embed] });
374.   } catch (error) {
375.     await interaction.editReply({
376.       content: `вқҢ Failed to fetch balance: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error'}`,
377.     });
378.   }
379. }
380. 
381. async function handlePending(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
382.   const pending = getPendingTips(interaction.user.id);
383.   
384.   if (pending.length === 0) {
385.     await interaction.reply({
386.       content: 'рҹ“Ӣ You have no pending tips.',
387.       ephemeral: true,
388.     });
389.     return;
390.   }
391. 
392.   const embed = new EmbedBuilder()
393.     .setColor(0x0099FF)
394.     .setTitle('рҹ“Ӣ Pending Tips')
395.     .setDescription('These tips were sent to you before you registered your wallet.')
396.     .addFields(
397.       pending.map(tip => ({
398.         name: `${tip.amount} SOL`,
399.         value: `From: <@${tip.senderId}>\nExpires: <t:${Math.floor(tip.expiresAt / 1000)}:R>`,
400.         inline: false
401.       }))
402.     );
403. 
404.   await interaction.reply({ embeds: [embed], ephemeral: true });
405. }
406.
```

</details>

```
1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. /**
3.  * Command Handler
4.  * 
5.  * Loads and manages slash commands.
6.  */
7. 
8. import { Collection } from 'discord.js';
9. import type { Command, CommandCollection } from '../types.js';
10. import * as commands from '../commands/index.js';
11. import { loadCommands as dynamicLoadCommands } from '../commands/loader.js';
12. 
13. export class CommandHandler {
14.   private commands: CommandCollection;
15. 
16.   constructor() {
17.     this.commands = new Collection();
18.   }
19. 
20.   /**
21.    * Load all commands
22.    */
23.   loadCommands(): void {
24.     const serviceId = process.env.SERVICE_ID || 'tiltcheck-bot';
25. 
26.     // Define which commands belong to which bot
27.     const dadBotCommands = ['dad', 'poker', 'help'];
28.     const tiltCheckBotCommands = ['tiltcheck', 'tip', 'airdrop', 'lockvault', 'casino', 'triviadrop', 'support', 'terms', 'dashboard', 'help'];
29. 
30.     const allowedCommands = serviceId === 'tiltcheck-dad-bot' 
31.       ? dadBotCommands 
32.       : tiltCheckBotCommands;
33. 
34.     // Load commands from the commands directory
35.     const commandModules = Object.values(commands);
36. 
37.     for (const command of commandModules) {
38.       if ('data' in command && 'execute' in command) {
39.         const cmdName = command.data.name;
40. 
41.         if (allowedCommands.includes(cmdName)) {
42.           this.commands.set(cmdName, command as Command);
43.           console.log(`  рҹ“„ /${cmdName}`);
44.         }
45.       }
46.     }
47. 
48.     console.log(`  в””в”Җв”Җ ${this.commands.size} commands loaded for ${serviceId}`);
49.   }
50. 
51.   /**
52.    * Get a command by name
53.    */
54.   getCommand(name: string): Command | undefined {
55.     return this.commands.get(name);
56.   }
57. 
58.   /**
59.    * Get all commands
60.    */
61.   getAllCommands(): Command[] {
62.     return Array.from(this.commands.values());
63.   }
64. 
65.   /**
66.    * Get command data for registration
67.    */
68.   getCommandData() {
69.     return this.getAllCommands().map((cmd) => cmd.data.toJSON());
70.   }
71. 
72.   /**
73.    * Dynamically discover and load all command files from the commands/
74.    * directory using the fs.readdir-based loader. This supplements (and
75.    * may replace) the static `loadCommands()` barrel import approach.
76.    *
77.    * After this resolves, the internal collection is replaced with the
78.    * dynamically-discovered set.
79.    */
80.   async loadCommandsDynamic(): Promise<void> {
81.     const discovered = await dynamicLoadCommands();
82.     this.commands = discovered as unknown as CommandCollection;
83.     console.log(`  [CommandHandler] Dynamic load complete вҖ“ ${this.commands.size} command(s) active`);
84.   }
85. }
```

1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. /**
3.  * Set Promo Channel Command (Mod Only)
4.  * Configure the channel where promo submissions are posted
5.  */
6. 
7. import { SlashCommandBuilder, ChatInputCommandInteraction, PermissionFlagsBits, ChannelType } from 'discord.js';
8. import { successEmbed, errorEmbed } from '@tiltcheck/discord-utils';
9. import type { Command } from '../types.js';
10. 
11. // In-memory storage for promo channel config (per guild)
12. // In production, this should be persisted to a database
13. const promoChannels = new Map<string, string>();
14. 
15. export function getPromoChannel(guildId: string): string | undefined {
16.   return promoChannels.get(guildId);
17. }
18. 
19. export const setpromochannel: Command = {
20.   data: new SlashCommandBuilder()
21.     .setName('setpromochannel')
22.     .setDescription('Set the channel for promo submissions (mods only)')
23.     .addChannelOption(option =>
24.       option
25.         .setName('channel')
26.         .setDescription('The channel to post promo submissions')
27.         .addChannelTypes(ChannelType.GuildText)
28.         .setRequired(true)
29.     )
30.     .setDefaultMemberPermissions(PermissionFlagsBits.ManageChannels) as unknown as SlashCommandBuilder,
31. 
32.   async execute(interaction: ChatInputCommandInteraction) {
33.     // Check if in a guild
34.     if (!interaction.guild) {
35.       await interaction.reply({
36.         embeds: [errorEmbed('Server Only', 'This command can only be used in a server.')],
37.         ephemeral: true,
38.       });
39.       return;
40.     }
41. 
42.     // Check permissions
43.     const member = interaction.member;
44.     if (!member || typeof member.permissions === 'string') {
45.       await interaction.reply({
46.         embeds: [errorEmbed('Permission Error', 'Unable to verify permissions.')],
47.         ephemeral: true,
48.       });
49.       return;
50.     }
51. 
52.     const channel = interaction.options.getChannel('channel', true);
53. 
54.     // Store the promo channel for this guild
55.     promoChannels.set(interaction.guild.id, channel.id);
56. 
57.     await interaction.reply({
58.       embeds: [successEmbed(
59.         'вң… Promo Channel Set',
60.         `Promo submissions will now be posted in <#${channel.id}>`
61.       )],
62.     });
63.   },
64. };
65.
```

C:\Users\jmeni\tiltcheck-monorepo/apps/discord-bot/src/commands/loader.ts

<details>
<summary>135 lines</summary>

```
1. /* Copyright (c) 2026 TiltCheck. All rights reserved. */
2. /**
3.  * Command Loader
4.  *
5.  * Dynamically discovers and loads all command modules from the commands/
6.  * directory using fs.readdir + dynamic import(). Each module must export:
7.  *   - `data`    вҖ“ a SlashCommandBuilder (or compatible) instance
8.  *   - `execute` вҖ“ a ChatInputCommandInteraction handler
9.  *
10.  * Also exports `registerCommands` which deploys the loaded commands to
11.  * Discord via the REST API (guild-scoped when guildId is provided, or
12.  * globally otherwise).
13.  */
14. 
15. import path from 'path';
16. import { fileURLToPath, pathToFileURL } from 'url';
17. import { Collection, REST, Routes } from 'discord.js';
18. import type { Command } from '../types.js';
19. 
20. // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
21. // Resolve the commands directory at runtime.
22. // import.meta.url is used here because this file lives inside commands/
23. // and we need to walk the same directory.
24. // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
25. const __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
26. const __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
27. 
28. /**
29.  * Loads commands from the barrel index (index.ts) rather than scanning
30.  * the directory. This ensures only explicitly exported commands are
31.  * registered вҖ” command files that exist on disk but aren't exported
32.  * from the index will be ignored.
33.  *
34.  * @returns A discord.js Collection keyed by command name.
35.  */
36. export async function loadCommands(): Promise<Collection<string, Command>> {
37.   const collection = new Collection<string, Command>();
38. 
39.   let mod: Record<string, unknown>;
40.   try {
41.     const indexPath = pathToFileURL(path.join(__dirname, 'index.js')).href;
42.     mod = await import(indexPath);
43.   } catch (err) {
44.     console.error('[CommandLoader] Failed to import command index:', err);
45.     return collection;
46.   }
47. 
48.   for (const [key, candidate] of Object.entries(mod)) {
49.     if (isCommand(candidate)) {
50.       const name: string = (candidate.data as { name: string }).name;
51.       if (collection.has(name)) {
52.         console.warn(`[CommandLoader] Duplicate command name "${name}" (export: ${key}) вҖ“ skipping`);
53.         continue;
54.       }
55.       collection.set(name, candidate);
56.       console.log(`  [CommandLoader] Loaded /${name}`);
57.     }
58.   }
59. 
60.   console.log(`[CommandLoader] ${collection.size} command(s) discovered.`);
61.   return collection;
62. }
63. 
64. /**
65.  * Deploys the provided commands to Discord via the REST API.
66.  *
67.  * - When `guildId` is supplied the commands are registered to that guild
68.  *   immediately (useful for development / staging).
69.  * - When `guildId` is omitted commands are registered globally (can take
70.  *   up to one hour to propagate).
71.  *
72.  * @param clientId - Discord application / client ID
73.  * @param guildId  - Optional guild ID for scoped (faster) deployment
74.  * @param token    - Bot token used to authenticate the REST call
75.  * @param commands - Collection returned by `loadCommands()`. When omitted
76.  *                   the loader will auto-discover commands before deploying.
77.  */
78. export async function registerCommands(
79.   clientId: string,
80.   guildId: string | undefined,
81.   token: string,
82.   commands?: Collection<string, Command>
83. ): Promise<void> {
84.   const cmdCollection = commands ?? (await loadCommands());
85. 
86.   if (cmdCollection.size === 0) {
87.     console.warn('[CommandLoader] No commands found вҖ“ skipping deployment.');
88.     return;
89.   }
90. 
91.   const body = Array.from(cmdCollection.values()).map((cmd) => cmd.data.toJSON());
92. 
93.   const rest = new REST({ version: '10' }).setToken(token);
94. 
95.   try {
96.     if (guildId) {
97.       console.log(`[CommandLoader] Deploying ${body.length} command(s) to guild ${guildId}вҖҰ`);
98.       await rest.put(Routes.applicationGuildCommands(clientId, guildId), { body });
99.       console.log('[CommandLoader] Guild commands deployed successfully.');
100.     } else {
101.       console.log(`[CommandLoader] Deploying ${body.length} command(s) globallyвҖҰ`);
102.       await rest.put(Routes.applicationCommands(clientId), { body });
103.       console.log('[CommandLoader] Global commands deployed successfully.');
104.     }
105. 
106.     for (const [name] of cmdCollection) {
107.       console.log(`  /${name}`);
108.     }
109.   } catch (err) {
110.     console.error('[CommandLoader] Failed to register commands with Discord:', err);
111.     throw err;
112.   }
113. }
114. 
115. // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
116. // Internal helpers
117. // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
118. 
119. /**
120.  * Type guard вҖ“ returns true when `value` looks like a valid Command object.
121.  */
122. function isCommand(value: unknown): value is Command {
123.   if (typeof value !== 'object' || value === null) return false;
124.   const v = value as Record<string, unknown>;
125.   return (
126.     'data' in v &&
127.     typeof v['data'] === 'object' &&
128.     v['data'] !== null &&
129.     'name' in (v['data'] as object) &&
130.     typeof (v['data'] as Record<string, unknown>)['name'] === 'string' &&
131.     'execute' in v &&
132.     typeof v['execute'] === 'function'
133.   );
134. }
135.
```

</details>

## **PART 9: CODE FIXES - EXAMPLES**

### **Fix 1: Remove Emoji from ping.ts**

```typescript
// BEFORE
const embed = successEmbed(
  'рҹҸ“ Pong!',
  `Bot latency: ${latency}ms\nWebSocket: ${interaction.client.ws.ping}ms`
);

// AFTER
const embed = successEmbed(
  'Pong',
  `Bot latency: ${latency}ms\nWebSocket: ${interaction.client.ws.ping}ms`
);
embed.setFooter({ text: 'Made for Degens. By Degens.' });
```

### **Fix 2: Standardize Footer (all commands)**

```typescript
// Add to ALL embed creations:
embed.setFooter({ text: 'Made for Degens. By Degens.' });
```

### **Fix 3: Fix buddy.ts tone**

```typescript
// BEFORE
if (targetUser.id === interaction.user.id) {
  await interaction.reply({ content: 'Seriously? You can't be your own damn buddy. Pick someone else.', ephemeral: true });
  return;
}

// AFTER
if (targetUser.id === interaction.user.id) {
  await interaction.reply({ content: 'You cannot add yourself as a buddy.', ephemeral: true });
  return;
}
```

### **Fix 4: Fix juice.ts timeout**

```typescript
// BEFORE - 30 iterations, 5sec each = 2.5min timeout risk
for (let i = 0; i \< 30; i++) {
  const balance = await connection.getBalance(escrow.publicKey);
  if (balance \>= amountLamports) {
    isFunded = true;
    break;
  }
  await new Promise(r =\> setTimeout(r, 5000));
}

// AFTER - Use webhook listener or shorter timeout
// Option 1: Reduce to 12 iterations (60 sec)
for (let i = 0; i \< 12; i++) {
  const balance = await connection.getBalance(escrow.publicKey);
  if (balance \>= amountLamports) {
    isFunded = true;
    break;
  }
  if (i === 11) {
    await interaction.editReply({ 
      content: 'Escrow funding timed out. Juice drop cancelled.',
      components: [] 
    });
    return;
  }
  await new Promise(r =\> setTimeout(r, 5000));
}

// Option 2: Use webhook for async notification
```

### **Fix 5: Add error context**

```typescript
// BEFORE
catch (error) {
  console.error('[Casino] Error:', error);
  await interaction.editReply({ content: 'вқҢ Failed to fetch casino data.' });
}

// AFTER
catch (error) {
  const errorMsg = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error';
  console.error('[Casino] Error:', errorMsg);
  await interaction.editReply({ 
    content: `вқҢ Failed to fetch casino data: ${errorMsg || 'Try again.'}` 
  });
}
```

## **RECOMMENDATIONS**

1. **Create a shared footer constant:**
```typescript
// discord-utils or shared package
export const BRAND_FOOTER = { text: 'Made for Degens. By Degens.' };
```

2. **Add emoji linter to pre-commit hooks** - Flag any emoji characters in command descriptions

3. **Create brand compliance checklist** for PRs:
   - [ ] No emojis in descriptions
   - [ ] Footer set to "Made for Degens. By Degens."
   - [ ] Tone is blunt/direct (no apologies, "please", "sorry")
   - [ ] Error messages include context
   - [ ] Input validation present

4. **Standardize error handling pattern:**
```typescript
const errorMsg = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to process request';
console.error(`[Command] Error:`, errorMsg);
await interaction.reply({ content: `вқҢ ${errorMsg}`, ephemeral: true });
```

5. **Refactor duplicate commands:** Consolidate `scan.ts` + `suslink.ts` into single `/link scan` command

## **CONCLUSION**

The TiltCheck Discord bot has **functional commands but significant brand compliance gaps**:

- вң… **Strengths:** Command structure is solid, most have error handling, subcommand organization is clean
- вқҢ **Weaknesses:** 40+ emojis violate policy, 12+ missing/wrong footers, tone inconsistencies, some input validation gaps, async timeout risks

**Estimated Fix Time:** 4-6 hours (mostly mechanical: remove emojis, fix footers, rewrite descriptions)

**Compliance Risk:** MEDIUM - Policy violations are visible to users but not system-breaking

Read apps/chrome-extension/src/auth-bridge.js (search for chrome.storage.local.set around line 59-78)\n2. Wrap storage.set in Promise and wait for completion:\n   ```javascript\n   try {\n     await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {\n       chrome.storage.local.set({\n         authToken: data.token,\n         userData: data.user,\n       }, (err) => {\n         if (err) reject(err);\n         else resolve();\n       });\n     });\n     // Send ACK back to parent before closing\n     if (window.opener) {\n       window.opener.postMessage({ type: 'auth-bridge-ack' }, '*');\n     }\n   } catch (error) {\n     console.error('[auth-bridge] Storage write failed:', error);\n     // Retry once\n     setTimeout(() => { /* retry */ }, 100);\n   }\n   ```\n\n3. Update sidebar.ts polling to:\n   - Wait for 'auth-bridge-ack' message\n   - Or timeout after 2000ms and check storage anyway\n   - Add retry logic if first read returns undefined\n\n4. Add error logging for debugging\n\nAfter completing:\n- Update SQL: UPDATE todos SET status = 'done' WHERE id = 'oauth-fix-storage-race'\n- Return summary of changes and how ACK/retry logic works"

421.     }
422. 
423.     // Generate state for CSRF protection. Prefix helps recover source in callback if cookies are blocked.
424.     const statePrefix = source === 'extension' ? 'ext_' : 'web_';
425.     const state = `${statePrefix}${generateOAuthState()}`;
426. 
427.     // Store state in a short-lived cookie
428.     // NOTE: No domain parameter = same-site only. This allows extension OAuth to work in production
429.     // since extension content scripts cannot access domain-scoped cookies (e.g., domain: .tiltcheck.me).
430.     // The callback validates: (1) state matches cookie if present, OR (2) state prefix is valid (ext_/web_).
431.     res.cookie('oauth_state', state, {
432.       httpOnly: true,
433.       secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
434.       sameSite: 'lax',
435.       maxAge: 10 * 60 * 1000, // 10 minutes
436.     });
437. 
438.     // Store redirect URL if provided
439.     const redirectUrl = req.query.redirect as string;
440.     if (redirectUrl) {
441.       res.cookie('oauth_redirect', redirectUrl, {
442.         httpOnly: true,
443.         secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
444.         sameSite: 'lax',
445.         maxAge: 10 * 60 * 1000,
446.       });
447.     }
448. 
449.     // Store source if provided (e.g., 'extension')
450.     if (source) {
451.       res.cookie('oauth_source', source, {
452.         httpOnly: true,
453.         secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
454.         sameSite: 'lax',
455.         maxAge: 10 * 60 * 1000,
456.       });
457.     }
458. 
459.     // Optional extension opener origin for stricter postMessage targeting.
460.     const openerOrigin = getTrustedExtensionOrigin(req.query.opener_origin);
```
