````
- вң… Added extension ID validation:
  - Retrieves stored ID from cookie and incoming ID from query params
  - For extension source: validates `storedExtId === incomingExtId`
  - Rejects mismatches with clear error: *"Extension runtime ID mismatch. This may indicate an unauthorized extension..."*
  - Clears cookie after validation
  - Validates before checking `postMessageTarget` (defense-in-depth)

---

### **Validation Flow**

```
Extension Initiate OAuth
  вҶ“
config.ts: getExtensionId() gets chrome.runtime.id
  вҶ“
getDiscordLoginUrl() adds ext_id={id} to URL
  вҶ“
auth-bridge.js: Verifies ext_id param exists, injects if missing
  вҶ“
GET /auth/discord/login?ext_id={id}&source=extension
  вҶ“
API stores ext_id in oauth_extension_id cookie
  вҶ“
Redirect to Discord OAuth вҶ’ User authorizes
  вҶ“
Discord redirects back to /auth/discord/callback
  вҶ“
API retrieves:
  - storedExtId from cookie
  - incomingExtId from query param
  вҶ“
Validation:
  вң“ If IDs match OR only one exists вҶ’ proceed
  вң— If IDs differ вҶ’ reject with error
  вҶ“
Clear cookie + proceed to postMessage validation
```

---

### **Error Handling**

| Scenario | Error Message | HTTP Status |
|----------|---------------|-------------|
| Extension ID mismatch on callback | "Extension runtime ID mismatch. This may indicate an unauthorized extension..." | 400 |
| Missing postMessage target after valid ID | "Missing trusted extension origin..." | 400 (existing) |

---

### **Security Properties**

- **Prevents Runtime ID Spoofing**: Extension must send same ID at login and callback
- **Resistant to Extension Reinstalls**: ID mismatch is caught before session creation
- **Secure Cookie Transport**: `httpOnly`, `sameSite: lax`, 10-min expiration
- **Defense in Depth**: Extension ID validation + origin validation + state validation

---

### **Testing Recommendations**

1. **Happy Path**: New extension installation вҶ’ Discord connect вҶ’ verify session created
2. **Reinstall Scenario**: Uninstall/reinstall extension вҶ’ attempt Discord connect вҶ’ expect ID mismatch error with retry guidance
3. **Malicious Extension**: Attempt callback with different `ext_id` вҶ’ expect rejection
4. **No Extension ID**: Older clients without ID param вҶ’ gracefully proceed (backward compatible)

---

**Status**: вң… Ready for deployment | All files modified with copyright headers intact | No build dependencies changed
````

</details>

### в„№пёҸ Notification

Background agent "Fix user-dashboard token exposure" (general-purpose) completed

<details>
<summary>Detail</summary>

Fix the JWT token exposure vulnerability in apps/user-dashboard/src/index.ts OAuth callback.

PROBLEM: JWT token is passed as URL query parameter (res.redirect(`/dashboard?token=${token}`)), exposing it in:
- Browser history
- Referer headers
- Browser logs
- Third-party logging

SOLUTION: Use Set-Cookie header + redirect pattern instead.

IMPLEMENTATION:
1. Read apps/user-dashboard/src/index.ts (search for the callback handler around line 136-174)
2. Instead of passing token in URL, set it as an HTTP-only secure cookie:
   ```javascript
   res.cookie('auth_token', token, {
     httpOnly: true,
     secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
     sameSite: 'lax',
     maxAge: 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000, // 7 days
   });
   res.redirect('/dashboard');
   ```
3. Update the dashboard frontend to read from cookie instead of URL param
4. Add security header: "Secure" flag for HTTPS
5. Verify no token is exposed in console/history

IMPORTANT: Also check apps/user-dashboard/src/ for any code that reads ?token= from URL and replace with cookie reading

After completing:
- Update SQL: UPDATE todos SET status = 'done' WHERE id = 'oauth-fix-token-exposure'
- Return summary of files changed and cookie configuration used

<sub>вҸұпёҸ 22m 49s</sub>

### в„№пёҸ Notification

Background agent "Fix extension storage race condition" (general-purpose) completed

<details>
<summary>Detail</summary>

Fix the chrome extension storage race condition in apps/chrome-extension/src/

PROBLEM: 
- auth-bridge.js writes to chrome.storage.local asynchronously
- sidebar.ts polls every 1000ms looking for authToken
- auth-bridge.js auto-closes after 1200ms
- If polling reads before write completes, auth fails silently

SOLUTION: Use Promise.all() to wait for storage write before closing, add retry logic and ACK messages.

IMPLEMENTATION:
1. Read apps/chrome-extension/src/auth-bridge.js (search for chrome.storage.local.set around line 59-78)
2. Wrap storage.set in Promise and wait for completion:
   ```javascript
   try {
     await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
       chrome.storage.local.set({
         authToken: data.token,
         userData: data.user,
       }, (err) => {
         if (err) reject(err);
         else resolve();
       });
     });
     // Send ACK back to parent before closing
     if (window.opener) {
       window.opener.postMessage({ type: 'auth-bridge-ack' }, '*');
     }
   } catch (error) {
     console.error('[auth-bridge] Storage write failed:', error);
     // Retry once
     setTimeout(() => { /* retry */ }, 100);
   }
   ```

3. Update sidebar.ts polling to:
   - Wait for 'auth-bridge-ack' message
   - Or timeout after 2000ms and check storage anyway
   - Add retry logic if first read returns undefined

4. Add error logging for debugging

After completing:
- Update SQL: UPDATE todos SET status = 'done' WHERE id = 'oauth-fix-storage-race'
- Return summary of changes and how ACK/retry logic works

</details>
